# math.NA [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Structure-preserving deflation of critical eigenvalues in quadratic eigenvalue problems associated with damped mass-spring systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16024)
*Rafikul Alam,Volker Mehrmann,Ninoslav Truhar*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文针对阻尼质量-弹簧系统的二次矩阵多项式，提出了保结构的特征值紧缩策略，通过修剪的保结构线性化来处理临界特征值（无穷大、零值和虚轴上的特征值），并分析了参数阻尼矩阵对纯虚特征值的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在阻尼质量-弹簧系统的二次矩阵多项式中，存在三种类型的临界特征值（无穷大、零值和虚轴上的特征值），这些特征值位于（鲁棒）稳定特征值集合的边界上。为了提高数值方法的效率和稳定性分析的准确性，需要在计算其他特征值和特征向量之前，通过将矩阵多项式投影到低维子空间来紧缩这些临界特征值。

Method: 提出保结构的紧缩策略，通过修剪的保结构线性化（trimmed structure-preserving linearization）来紧缩临界特征值。将这些方法应用于双曲问题的特殊情况，并分析（可能是低秩的）参数阻尼矩阵对纯虚特征值的影响。

Result: 成功开发了能够有效处理阻尼质量-弹簧系统中临界特征值的保结构紧缩方法。该方法能够在保持系统结构特性的同时，将问题降维到更易处理的子空间。对于双曲问题和参数阻尼矩阵的分析提供了理论基础和实用指导。

Conclusion: 通过保结构的紧缩策略和修剪的保结构线性化，可以有效处理阻尼质量-弹簧系统中的临界特征值问题。这种方法不仅提高了数值计算的效率，还为鲁棒稳定性分析提供了可靠的工具，特别是在处理双曲问题和分析参数阻尼矩阵影响方面具有重要价值。

Abstract: For a quadratic matrix polynomial associated with a damped mass-spring system
there are three types of critical eigenvalues, the eigenvalues $\infty$ and $0$
and the eigenvalues on the imaginary axis. All these are on the boundary of the
set of (robustly) stable eigenvalues. For numerical methods, but also for
(robust) stability analysis, it is desirable to deflate such eigenvalues by
projecting the matrix polynomial to a lower dimensional subspace before
computing the other eigenvalues and eigenvectors. We describe
structure-preserving deflation strategies that deflate these eigenvalues via a
trimmed structure-preserving linearization. We employ these results for the
special case of hyperbolic problems. We also analyze the effect of a (possibly
low rank) parametric damping matrix on purely imaginary eigenvalues.

</details>


### [2] [Diff-ANO: Towards Fast High-Resolution Ultrasound Computed Tomography via Conditional Consistency Models and Adjoint Neural Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16344)
*Xiang Cao,Qiaoqiao Ding,Xinliang Liu,Lei Zhang,Xiaoqun Zhang*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了Diff-ANO框架，结合条件一致性模型和伴随算子学习来解决超声计算断层成像(USCT)中的非线性逆问题，显著提升了计算效率和重建质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的亥姆霍兹方程约束USCT方法在集成扩散生成先验时面临三个基本挑战：PDE约束梯度计算、离散化引起的近似误差，以及神经网络与数值PDE求解器之间的计算不平衡问题。

Method: 提出Diff-ANO框架，包含两个关键创新：(1)条件一致性模型，通过直接学习扩散轨迹的自一致映射实现测量条件下的少步采样；(2)伴随算子学习模块，用神经算子代理替代传统PDE求解器进行高效的基于伴随的梯度计算。引入批量收敛Born级数(BCBS)作为内存高效的在线神经算子训练对生成策略。

Result: 综合实验表明，Diff-ANO在计算效率和重建质量方面都有显著改善，特别是在稀疏视图和部分视图测量场景下表现优异。

Conclusion: Diff-ANO成功解决了传统USCT方法的三个核心挑战，为超声计算断层成像提供了一个高效且高质量的解决方案，在实际部署中具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: Ultrasound Computed Tomography (USCT) constitutes a nonlinear inverse problem
with inherent ill-posedness that can benefit from regularization through
diffusion generative priors. However, traditional approaches for solving
Helmholtz equation-constrained USCT face three fundamental challenges when
integrating these priors: PDE-constrained gradient computation,
discretization-induced approximation errors, and computational imbalance
between neural networks and numerical PDE solvers. In this work, we introduce
\textbf{Diff-ANO} (\textbf{Diff}usion-based Models with \textbf{A}djoint
\textbf{N}eural \textbf{O}perators), a novel framework that combines
conditional consistency models with adjoint operator learning to address these
limitations. Our two key innovations include: (1) a \textit{conditional
consistency model} that enables measurement-conditional few-step sampling by
directly learning a self-consistent mapping from diffusion trajectories, and
(2) an \textit{adjoint operator learning} module that replaces traditional PDE
solvers with neural operator surrogates for efficient adjoint-based gradient
computation. To enable practical deployment, we introduce the batch-based
Convergent Born Series (BCBS)--a memory-efficient strategy for online
generation of neural operator training pairs. Comprehensive experiments
demonstrate that Diff-ANO significantly improves both computational efficiency
and reconstruction quality, especially under sparse-view and partial-view
measurement scenarios.

</details>


### [3] [Neural Network Acceleration of Iterative Methods for Nonlinear Schrödinger Eigenvalue Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16349)
*Daniel Peterseim,Jan-F. Pietschmann,Jonas Püschel,Kilian Ruess*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种使用神经网络加速求解非线性薛定谔特征值问题的新方法，通过预测和优化解轨迹来提高收敛速度和精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统求解器在极端参数条件下（如旋转玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚态问题）收敛速度慢，需要开发更高效的数值方法来解决非线性特征向量问题。

Method: 使用神经网络预测和改进解轨迹，利用先前仿真的知识来加速迭代方法求解非线性薛定谔特征值问题。

Result: 数值实验表明该方法相比传统求解器实现了显著的速度提升，同时展现了方法的优势和局限性。

Conclusion: 神经网络辅助的求解方法能够有效加速非线性特征值问题的求解，为量子力学等领域的计算问题提供了新的解决思路。

Abstract: We present a novel approach to accelerate iterative methods to solve
nonlinear Schr\"odinger eigenvalue problems using neural networks. Nonlinear
eigenvector problems are fundamental in quantum mechanics and other fields, yet
conventional solvers often suffer from slow convergence in extreme parameter
regimes, as exemplified by the rotating Bose- Einstein condensate (BEC)
problem. Our method uses a neural network to predict and refine solution
trajectories, leveraging knowledge from previous simulations to improve
convergence speed and accuracy. Numerical experiments demonstrate significant
speed-up over classical solvers, highlighting both the strengths and
limitations of the approach.

</details>


### [4] [Entropic approximations of the semigeostrophic shallow water equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16415)
*Jean-David Benamou,Colin J. Cotter,Jacob J. M. Francis,Hugo Malamut*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文基于最优传输理论，提出了半地转旋转浅水方程的离散化方法，使用Moreau-Yoshida正则化处理Wasserstein度量，并开发了求解时间依赖浅水问题的迭代算法


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半地转旋转浅水方程的数值求解存在困难，需要基于最优传输理论发展新的离散化方法来更好地处理这类地球物理流体动力学问题

Method: 采用最优传输公式化的Moreau-Yoshida正则化方法对Wasserstein度量进行处理；提出熵正则化版本的旋转浅水方程；用加权Dirac测度的和来离散化测度，近似层深度的L2范数；开发迭代算法求解两个测度之间的离散优化问题

Result: 成功构建了半地转旋转浅水方程的离散化格式，提出的迭代方法具有收敛性，并通过数值算例验证了方法的有效性，能够求解时间依赖的浅水问题

Conclusion: 基于最优传输理论的离散化方法为半地转旋转浅水方程提供了新的数值求解途径，所提出的迭代算法收敛性良好，为地球物理流体动力学数值模拟提供了有效工具

Abstract: We develop a discretisation of the semigeostrophic rotating shallow water
equations, based upon their optimal transport formulation. This takes the form
of a Moreau-Yoshida regularisation of the Wasserstein metric. Solutions of the
optimal transport formulation provide the shallow water layer depth represented
as a measure, which is itself the push forward of an evolving measure under the
semigeostrophic coordinate transformation. First, we propose and study an
entropy regularised version of the rotating shallow water equations. Second, we
discretise the regularised problem by replacing both measures with weighted
sums of Dirac measures, and approximate the (squared) L2 norm of the layer
depth, which defines the potential energy. We propose an iterative method to
solve the discrete optimisation problem relating the two measures, and analyse
its convergence. The iterative method is demonstrated numerically and applied
to the solution of the time-dependent shallow water problem in numerical
examples.

</details>


### [5] [On finite precision block Lanczos computations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16484)
*Dorota Šimonová,Petr Tichý*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文将Greenbaum在1989年对有限精度Lanczos算法的数学模型扩展到块Lanczos算法，通过构造扰动完成延拓过程，并建立了块三对角矩阵可解释为精确块Lanczos算法应用于更大模型矩阵的理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Greenbaum在1989年为单向量Lanczos算法建立了有限精度计算的数学模型，但这一理论框架尚未扩展到块Lanczos算法。需要建立块情况下的类似理论模型，以更好地理解和分析块Lanczos算法在有限精度下的行为。

Method: 将Greenbaum的单向量延拓过程推广到块情况，通过精心构造的扰动在有限步内完成延拓过程。推导出保证所需扰动保持较小的充分条件，确保模型矩阵的特征值与原矩阵特征值保持接近。建立了k次迭代后产生的块三对角矩阵可解释为精确块Lanczos算法应用于更大模型矩阵的理论框架。

Result: 成功将Greenbaum的理论扩展到块Lanczos算法，建立了相应的数学模型。推导出了保证扰动较小的充分条件。通过数值实验验证了延拓过程的实际实现，并empirically评估了充分条件的有效性和扰动的大小。发现与单向量情况不同，块情况下充分条件是否总能满足仍是一个开放问题。

Conclusion: 成功建立了有限精度块Lanczos算法的数学模型，为理解其数值行为提供了理论基础。虽然推导出了保证扰动较小的充分条件，但与单向量情况不同，这些条件在块情况下是否总能满足还需要进一步研究。数值实验验证了理论的实用性。

Abstract: In her seminal 1989 work, Greenbaum demonstrated that the results produced by
the finite precision Lanczos algorithm after $k$ iterations can be interpreted
as exact Lanczos results applied to a larger matrix, whose eigenvalues lie in
small intervals around those of the original matrix. This establishes a
mathematical model for finite precision Lanczos computations. In this paper, we
extend these ideas to the block Lanczos algorithm. We generalize the
continuation process and show that it can be completed in a finite number of
iterations using carefully constructed perturbations. The block tridiagonal
matrices produced after $k$ iterations can then be interpreted as arising from
the exact block Lanczos algorithm applied to a larger model matrix. We derive
sufficient conditions under which the required perturbations remain small,
ensuring that the eigenvalues of the model matrix stay close to those of the
original matrix. While in the single-vector case these conditions are always
satisfiable, as shown by Greenbaum based on results by Paige, the question of
whether they can always be satisfied in the block case remains open. Finally,
we present numerical experiments demonstrating a practical implementation of
the continuation process and empirically assess the validity of the sufficient
conditions and the size of the perturbations.

</details>


### [6] [Neumann series of Bessel functions in direct and inverse spherically symmetric transmission eigenvalue problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16554)
*Vladislav V. Kravchenko,L. Estefania Murcia-Lozano,Nikolaos Pallikarakis*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新颖的贝塞尔函数诺依曼级数(NSBF)方法来解决球对称域中变折射率的传输特征值问题，该方法可以处理实数和复数特征值，并在直接和逆问题求解中都表现出高精度和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传输特征值问题在逆散射理论中起核心作用，但在具有变折射率的球对称域中，同时处理实数和复数特征值的直接和逆问题的数值求解仍然具有挑战性。现有方法在计算精度和鲁棒性方面存在局限性。

Method: 通过Liouville变换将传输特征值问题重新表述为Sturm-Liouville方程，然后将其特征函数展开为贝塞尔函数诺依曼级数(NSBF)，其系数通过简单的递归积分计算。对于直接问题，通过在截断的NSBF部分和上进行根查找来求解特征值；对于逆问题，采用两步方法：首先通过新的NSBF算法从谱数据中恢复变换区间长度δ，然后通过求解线性系统重构折射率n(r)。

Result: 数值算例表明该方法在各种折射率范围内都具有鲁棒性和高精度。对于直接问题，使用少量系数就能获得高精度的实数或复数特征值。对于逆问题，成功实现了折射率的重构，且对δ或对比度1-n(r)的符号没有先验假设要求。还实现了谱补全技术来处理特征值数据有限的情况。

Conclusion: NSBF方法为求解球对称域中变折射率的传输特征值问题提供了一种有效的数值工具，在直接和逆问题求解中都表现出优异的性能，为逆散射理论的实际应用提供了新的技术途径。

Abstract: The transmission eigenvalue problem (TEP) plays a central role in inverse
scattering theory. Despite substantial theoretical progress, the numerical
solution of direct and inverse TEP in spherically symmetric domains with
variable refractive index covering real and complex eigenvalues remains
challenging. This study introduces a novel Neumann Series of Bessel Functions
(NSBF) methodology to address this challenge. After reformulating the TEP as a
Sturm-Liouville equation via a Liouville transformation, we expand its
characteristic function in an NSBF whose coefficients are computed by simple
recursive integration. In the direct problem, eigenvalues real or complex are
found by root finding on a truncated NSBF partial sum, yielding high accuracy
with a few coefficients, as demonstrated with various examples. For the inverse
problem, we develop a two-step approach: first, recovering the transformed
interval length $\delta$ from spectral data via a new NSBF-based algorithm, and
second, reconstructing the refractive index $n(r)$ by solving a linear system
for the first NSBF coefficients. A spectrum completion technique is also
implemented to complete the spectrum and solve the corresponding inverse
problem when eigenvalue data is limited. Numerical examples confirm the
method's robustness and accuracy across a wide range of refractive indices,
with no a priori assumptions on $\delta$ or the sign of the contrast $1-n(r)$.

</details>


### [7] [Data-Driven Adaptive Gradient Recovery for Unstructured Finite Volume Computations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16571)
*G. de Romémont,F. Renac,F. Chinesta,J. Nunez,D. Gueyffier*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于数据驱动的方法，通过改进的DeepONet架构来增强非结构化有限体积方法中的梯度重构，专门用于求解2D欧拉方程等双曲守恒律。该方法结合了局部几何信息和物理约束正则化，在保持稳定性和守恒性的同时，相比传统二阶有限体积格式实现了20-60%的精度提升和更高的计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的二阶有限体积方法在非结构化网格上求解双曲守恒律（如2D欧拉方程）时，在激波主导区域的梯度重构精度有限，且在复杂几何配置下的计算效率和精度需要进一步提升。因此需要开发新的数据驱动方法来改进梯度重构，以获得更高的求解精度和计算效率。

Method: 采用改进的DeepONet架构，将局部几何信息融入神经网络，利用局部网格拓扑确保旋转不变性，并保证学习算子的一阶约束。训练方法结合了物理信息正则化，包括熵惩罚、总变差递减惩罚和参数正则化。模型在高保真数据集上训练，该数据集来源于正弦波和随机分段常数初始条件的周期边界条件解。

Result: 在文献中的验证测试案例（包括挑战性几何配置）上，相比传统二阶有限体积格式实现了显著的精度改善，解精度提升20-60%，同时增强了计算效率。收敛性研究显示相比传统求解器具有更好的网格收敛率。该算法比传统二阶有限体积求解器更快且更精确。

Conclusion: 提出的算法能够在更粗糙的网格上实现高保真仿真，同时保持双曲守恒律所必需的稳定性和守恒性质。这项工作代表了新一代求解器的发展方向，即将机器学习工具与传统数值格式相结合，同时确保结果满足物理约束，为计算流体力学提供了更高效和精确的求解方案。

Abstract: We present a novel data-driven approach for enhancing gradient reconstruction
in unstructured finite volume methods for hyperbolic conservation laws,
specifically for the 2D Euler equations. Our approach extends previous
structured-grid methodologies to unstructured meshes through a modified
DeepONet architecture that incorporates local geometry in the neural network.
The architecture employs local mesh topology to ensure rotation invariance,
while also ensuring first-order constraint on the learned operator. The
training methodology incorporates physics-informed regularization through
entropy penalization, total variation diminishing penalization, and parameter
regularization to ensure physically consistent solutions, particularly in
shock-dominated regions. The model is trained on high-fidelity datasets
solutions derived from sine waves and randomized piecewise constant initial
conditions with periodic boundary conditions, enabling robust generalization to
complex flow configurations or geometries. Validation test cases from the
literature, including challenging geometry configuration, demonstrates
substantial improvements in accuracy compared to traditional second-order
finite volume schemes. The method achieves gains of 20-60% in solution accuracy
while enhancing computational efficiency. A convergence study has been conveyed
and reveal improved mesh convergence rates compared to the conventional solver.
The proposed algorithm is faster and more accurate than the traditional
second-order finite volume solver, enabling high-fidelity simulations on
coarser grids while preserving the stability and conservation properties
essential for hyperbolic conservation laws. This work is a part of a new
generation of solvers that are built by combining Machine-Learning (ML) tools
with traditional numerical schemes, all while ensuring physical constraint on
the results.

</details>


### [8] [A Conservative and Positivity-Preserving Discontinuous Galerkin Method for the Population Balance Equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16631)
*Ziyao Xu,Guanyang Liu,Yong-Tao Zhang*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种保守的、保正性的间断Galerkin方法来求解粒子平衡方程，该方程描述了由于生长、成核、聚集和破碎导致的粒子数在不同粒径上的分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的数值方法在求解粒子平衡方程时难以同时保证数量守恒、质量守恒和数密度的正性，特别是在处理聚集-破碎过程时，经典的Zhang-Shu限制器不能直接应用于保持一阶矩（局部质量）的正性。

Method: 设计了一种间断Galerkin方案，对生长和成核采用标准处理方法，对聚集和破碎引入新的离散化方法。生死项采用对称双积分形式离散化，使用积分域的公共细化和精心选择的求积规则进行计算。通过证明每个单元上一阶矩的正性，构建了保矩守恒限制器来强制整个域上的非负性。

Result: 数值结果验证了所提方法的精度、守恒性和鲁棒性。该方法成功实现了生长中的数量守恒、聚集和破碎中的质量守恒，以及聚集-破碎过程中数密度的正性保持。

Conclusion: 这是首个开发出既保持正性又守恒指定矩的算法。所提出的间断Galerkin方法为粒子平衡方程提供了一个准确、守恒且鲁棒的数值求解方案，特别是在处理复杂的聚集-破碎过程时表现出色。

Abstract: We develop a conservative, positivity-preserving discontinuous Galerkin (DG)
method for the population balance equation (PBE), which models the distribution
of particle numbers across particle sizes due to growth, nucleation,
aggregation, and breakage. To ensure number conservation in growth and mass
conservation in aggregation and breakage, we design a DG scheme that applies
standard treatment for growth and nucleation, and introduces a novel
discretization for aggregation and breakage. The birth and death terms are
discretized in a symmetric double-integral form, evaluated using a common
refinement of the integration domain and carefully selected quadrature rules.
Beyond conservation, we focus on preserving the positivity of the number
density in aggregation-breakage. Since local mass corresponds to the first
moment, the classical Zhang-Shu limiter, which preserves the zeroth moment
(cell average), is not directly applicable. We address this by proving the
positivity of the first moment on each cell and constructing a
moment-conserving limiter that enforces nonnegativity across the domain. To our
knowledge, this is the first work to develop a positivity-preserving algorithm
that conserves a prescribed moment. Numerical results verify the accuracy,
conservation, and robustness of the proposed method.

</details>

Abstract: In this paper, we propose and analyze an accurate numerical approach to

The proposed method exhibits superconvergence rates in the physical space

### [13] [The inverse initial data problem for anisotropic Navier-Stokes equations via Legendre time reduction method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16810)
*Cong B. Van,Thuy T. Le,Loc H. Nguyen*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于勒让德时间约简的新计算框架，用于从侧边界观测数据重构可压缩各向异性纳维-斯托克斯方程的初始速度场


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在流体内部状态无法直接测量的应用中，需要从边界观测数据重构初始速度场，这是一个重要的逆初值问题

Method: 引入基于勒让德时间约简的新计算框架，将速度场投影到时间上的指数加权勒让德基上，将原始的时间相关逆问题转化为耦合的时间无关椭圆系统，并使用皮卡迭代和稳定化最小二乘格式求解

Result: 二维数值实验证实该方法能够准确稳健地重构初始速度场，即使在存在显著测量噪声和复杂各向异性结构的情况下也表现良好

Abstract: We consider the inverse initial data problem for the compressible anisotropic
Navier-Stokes equations, where the goal is to reconstruct the initial velocity
field from lateral boundary observations. This problem arises in applications
where direct measurements of internal fluid states are unavailable. We
introduce a novel computational framework based on Legendre time reduction,
which projects the velocity field onto an exponentially weighted Legendre basis
in time. This transformation reduces the original time-dependent inverse
problem to a coupled, time-independent elliptic system. The resulting reduced
model is solved iteratively using a Picard iteration and a stabilized
least-squares formulation under noisy boundary data. Numerical experiments in
two dimensions confirm that the method accurately and robustly reconstructs
initial velocity fields, even in the presence of significant measurement noise
and complex anisotropic structures. This approach offers a flexible and
computationally tractable alternative for inverse modeling in fluid dynamics
with anisotropic media.

</details>

### [14] [The Intrinsic Riemannian Proximal Gradient Method for Convex Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16055)
*Ronny Bergmann,Hajg Jasa,Paula John,Max Pfeffer*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在哈达玛流形上求解测地凸优化问题的内在凸黎曼近端梯度方法，该方法直接在流形上操作而不需要嵌入或切空间，并证明了收敛性理论


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的黎曼优化方法通常需要在嵌入空间或切空间中操作，这增加了计算复杂度。本文旨在开发一种直接在流形上操作的内在方法，用于求解包含光滑和非光滑函数的测地凸优化问题

Method: 提出了内在凸黎曼近端梯度(CRPG)方法，该方法直接使用流形近端映射处理非光滑步骤，无需在嵌入空间或切空间中操作。方法建立在哈达玛流形的几何结构基础上

Result: 对于凸问题建立了次线性收敛率，对于强凸问题建立了线性收敛率。推导了推广欧几里得情况的基本近端梯度不等式。在双曲空间和对称正定矩阵流形上的数值实验显示相比现有方法有显著的计算优势

Conclusion: 所提出的CRPG方法为哈达玛流形上的测地凸优化提供了一个有效的内在求解框架，具有理论保证的收敛性和实际的计算优势，为黎曼优化领域提供了新的工具

Abstract: We consider a class of (possibly strongly) geodesically convex optimization
problems on Hadamard manifolds, where the objective function splits into the
sum of a smooth and a possibly nonsmooth function. We introduce an intrinsic
convex Riemannian proximal gradient (CRPG) method that employs the manifold
proximal map for the nonsmooth step, without operating in the embedding or
tangent space. A sublinear convergence rate for convex problems and a linear
convergence rate for strongly convex problems is established, and we derive
fundamental proximal gradient inequalities that generalize the Euclidean case.
Our numerical experiments on hyperbolic spaces and manifolds of symmetric
positive definite matrices demonstrate substantial computational advantages
over existing methods.

Result: 成功证明了协方差交集在所有保守无偏线性融合规则中的最优性适用于一般的两个无偏部分状态估计融合情况，提供了这些问题的一般可解性条件和最优解特征方程

Conclusion: 协方差交集方法在信息融合领域具有更广泛的最优性，三个等价优化问题为解决实际融合问题提供了多种途径，为信息融合理论奠定了更坚实的数学基础

Abstract: We show that Covariance Intersection (CI) is optimal amongst all conservative

much stronger result that three different optimization problems are equivalent,

problem with respect to a strictly isotone cost function, the scalar Covariance
Intersection (CI) problem, and a simple semi-definite program (SDP). We provide

characterizing the optimal solutions for the matrix determinant and matrix

  <summary>Details</summary>

guarantee -- certification of worst-case performance over all parameters within

training. The regularization term is derived from the performance estimation
problem (PEP) framework based on semidefinite programming, in which the

training to learn the hyperparameters for several first-order methods:

alternating direction method of multipliers. Through various numerical examples
from signal processing, control, and statistics, we demonstrate that the

iterations, while also maintaining strong robustness guarantees. Notably, our
approach is highly data-efficient in that we only use ten training instances in
all of the numerical examples.

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于广义特征值计算的层次化松弛方法，用于求解多项式约束集上多项式最小值的下界，相比传统凸松弛技术具有更好的可扩展性

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多项式优化问题的凸松弛技术存在计算复杂度高、难以处理大规模问题的局限性，需要一种更高效、可扩展的方法来获得多项式约束优化问题的下界

Method: 提出基于广义特征值计算的层次化可处理松弛方法，通过计算从问题数据导出的矩阵对的最小广义特征值来获得下界，构建嵌套的结构化凸外逼近序列

Result: 该方法适用于所有具有有界约束集的多项式优化问题，线性优化可简化为特征值计算，数值实验表明相比基于平方和非负性证书的凸松弛方法具有更好的可扩展性

Conclusion: 提出的基于广义特征值的层次化松弛框架为多项式优化问题提供了一种高效且可扩展的求解方法，特别适用于大规模问题实例，并且可以使用现成软件实现

Abstract: We present a hierarchy of tractable relaxations to obtain lower bounds on the
minimum value of a polynomial over a constraint set defined by polynomial
equations. In contrast to previous convex relaxation techniques for this
problem, our method is based on computing the smallest generalized eigenvalue
of a pair of matrices derived from the problem data, which can be accomplished
for large problem instances using off-the-shelf software. We characterize the
algebraic structure in a problem that facilitates the application of our
framework, and we observe that our method is applicable for all polynomial
optimization problems with bounded constraint sets. Our construction also
yields a nested sequence of structured convex outer approximations of a bounded
algebraic variety with the property that linear optimization over each
approximation reduces to an eigenvalue computation. Finally, we present
numerical experiments on representative problems in which we demonstrate the
scalability of our approach compared to convex relaxation methods derived from
sums-of-squares certificates of nonnegativity.

Abstract: This PhD thesis presents a distributional view of optimization in place of a
worst-case perspective. We motivate this view with an investigation of the
failure point of classical optimization. Subsequently we consider the

such a distributional view may explain predictable progress of optimization in
high dimension. It further turns out that this distributional view provides
insights into optimal step size control of gradient descent. To enable these
results, we develop mathematical tools to deal with random input to random

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注确定性系统，而实际应用中系统动态和成本函数往往具有随机性。本文旨在填补这一空白，研究同时考虑状态动态和成本函数随机性的博弈问题，这种随机性导致了复杂的全耦合交叉耦合随机Riccati方程结构。

Method: 采用状态反馈策略通过解耦由两个对称交叉耦合随机Riccati方程(CCREs)控制的随机哈密顿系统来刻画均衡。随机系数诱导出高阶非线性后向随机差分方程系统。使用动态规划原理构造解，将均衡策略与耦合Lyapunov型方程联系起来。

Result: 在最小正则性条件下，建立了闭环纳什均衡存在的充要条件，这些条件取决于CCREs的正则可解性，无需强假设。成功构造了均衡策略的解，并建立了与耦合Lyapunov型方程的联系。

Abstract: This paper investigates closed-loop Nash equilibria for discrete-time
linear-quadratic (LQ) stochastic nonzero-sum difference games with random
coefficients. Unlike existing works, we consider randomness in both state
dynamics and cost functionals, leading to a complex structure of fully coupled
cross-coupled stochastic Riccati equations (CCREs). The key contributions lie
in characterizing the equilibrium via state-feedback strategies derived by
decoupling stochastic Hamiltonian systems governed by two symmetric CCREs-these
random coefficients induce a higher-order nonlinear backward stochastic
difference equation (BS$\triangle$E) system, fundamentally differing from
deterministic counterparts. Under minimal regularity conditions, we establish
necessary and sufficient conditions for closed-loop Nash equilibrium existence,
contingent on the regular solvability of CCREs without requiring strong
assumptions. Solutions are constructed using a dynamic programming principle
(DPP), linking equilibrium strategies to coupled Lyapunov-type equations. Our
analysis resolves critical challenges in modeling inherent randomness and
provides a unified framework for dynamic decision-making under uncertainty.

Result: 第一种方法在Hölder度量次正则性和梯度局部Hölder连续性条件下实现局部超线性收敛；第二种方法在Lipschitz连续梯度假设下证明了全局收敛性，并得到O(ε^{-2})的最坏情况全局复杂度界。数值实验在生化反应网络、单调非线性方程和图像去模糊等问题上验证了算法效果。

search directions by solving the LM linear system inexactly, subject to
specific residual-based conditions. The first method uses an adaptive scheme to
update the LM parameter, and we establish its local superlinear convergence

Abstract: Topology optimization has emerged as a powerful and increasingly relevant
strategy for enhancing the flexibility and efficiency of power system
operations. However, solving these problems is computationally demanding due to
their combinatorial nature and the use of big-M formulations.
Optimization-based bound tightening (OBBT) is a well-known strategy to improve
the solution of mixed-integer linear programs (MILPs) by computing tighter
bounds for continuous variables. Yet, existing OBBT approaches in topology
optimization typically relax all switching decisions in the bounding
subproblems, leading to excessively loose feasible regions and limited bound
improvements. In this work, we propose a topology-aware bound tightening method
that uses network structure to determine which switching variables to relax.
Through extensive computational experiments on the IEEE 118-bus system, we find
that keeping a small subset of switching variables as binary, while relaxing
the rest, strikes a sweet spot between the computational effort required to
solve the bounding problems and the tightness of the resulting bounds.

### [27] [On the Worst-Case Analysis of Cyclic Block Coordinate Descent type Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16675)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 块坐标下降算法在实践中表现优异，但其最坏情况行为尚未被完全理解，现有的收敛分析无法完全解释这些算法的实际成功，需要更深入的理论分析来填补这一空白。

Method: 将性能估计问题(PEP)方法扩展到坐标光滑凸函数，提出必要的插值条件，并利用此方法分析三种不同的BCD算法：循环坐标下降(CCD)、交替最小化(AM)和循环加速坐标下降(CACD)。

Result: 获得了三种BCD算法更紧的数值上界，在某些情况下显著优于现有最佳界限；证明了CCD算法在更自然的凸优化假设下的收敛性；发现了CCD最坏情况相对于坐标光滑常数的尺度不变性；建立了CCD最坏情况性能的下界等于块数乘以全梯度下降在光滑凸函数类上的最坏情况。

Abstract: We study the worst-case behavior of Block Coordinate Descent (BCD) type
algorithms for unconstrained minimization of coordinate-wise smooth convex
functions. This behavior is indeed not completely understood, and the practical
success of these algorithms is not fully explained by current convergence
analyses. We extend the recently proposed Performance Estimation Problem (PEP)
approach to convex coordinate-wise smooth functions by proposing necessary
interpolation conditions. We then exploit this to obtain improved numerical
upper bounds on the worst-case convergence rate of three different BCD
algorithms, namely Cyclic Coordinate Descent (CCD), Alternating Minimization
(AM), and a Cyclic version of the Random Accelerated Coordinate Descent
introduced in Fercoq and Richt\'arik (2015) (CACD), substantially outperforming
the best current bounds in some situations. In addition, we show the
convergence of the CCD algorithm with more natural assumptions in the context
of convex optimization than those typically made in the literature. Our
methodology uncovers a number of phenomena, some of which can be formally
established. These include a scale-invariance property of the worst case of CCD
with respect to the coordinate-wise smoothness constants and a lower bound on
the worst-case performance of CCD which is equal to the number of blocks times
the worst-case of full gradient descent over the class of smooth convex
functions. We also adapt our framework to the analysis of random BCD
algorithms, and present numerical results showing that the standard
acceleration scheme in Fercoq and Richt\'arik (2015) appears to be inefficient
for deterministic algorithms.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析d维欧几里得空间开集上标量值光滑函数空间中加权复合算子的性质，建立不同动力学概念之间的等价性关系

Abstract: A weighted composition operator on the space of scalar-valued smooth
functions on an open set of d-dimensional Euclidean space is supercyclic if and
only if it is weakly mixing, and it is strongly supercyclic if and only if it
is mixing. Every mixing such operator is chaotic. In the one-dimensional case,
it is supercyclic if and only if it is mixing and if and only if it is chaotic.

spaces as an application.

t+\frac{1}{2}x'Ax+bx+c$ at infinity, with an explicitly derived convergence
rate. Furthermore, we investigate Dirichlet type problems with prescribed
asymptotic behavior, featuring two key innovations: applicability to all
dimensions $n\geq 2$, and no requirement for the matrix $A$ to be positive
definite or close to a scalar multiple of the identity matrix. These results
establish the relationship among Liouville type rigidity, asymptotic analysis
at infinity, and boundary value problems (including Dirichlet type and initial
value type).

### [39] [Trace and Observability Inequalities for Laplace Eigenfunctions on the Torus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16599)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典的Zygmund和Bourgain-Rudnick定理只适用于低维情况，需要将其推广到高维环面上的拉普拉斯特征函数，并建立更一般的迹不等式和可观测性不等式的刻画条件。这对于量子极限理论、薛定谔方程控制理论等应用具有重要意义。

Method: 结合多种数学工具：(1)球面上格点的聚类结构分析；(2)解耦估计技术；(3)构造具有强集中性或消失行为的特征函数，分别针对迹不等式和可观测性不等式进行定制化分析。通过测度的可积性、正则性以及支撑维数来建立充分和必要条件。

Result: 成功刻画了使迹不等式和可观测性不等式对所有拉普拉斯特征函数一致成立的Borel测度条件。基于测度的可积性和正则性给出了充分条件，基于测度支撑的维数给出了必要条件。将经典定理推广到了高维情形。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了高维环面上拉普拉斯特征函数迹不等式和可观测性不等式的完整理论框架，不仅推广了经典结果，还为Cantor-Lebesgue型定理、量子极限约束和薛定谔方程控制理论等领域提供了新的理论工具和应用基础。

Abstract: We investigate trace and observability inequalities for Laplace
eigenfunctions on the d-dimensional torus, with respect to arbitrary Borel
measures $\mu$. Specifically, we characterize the measures $\mu$ for which the
inequalities
  $$ \int |u|^2 d \mu \lesssim \int |u|^2 d x \quad \text{(trace)}, \qquad \int
|u|^2 d \mu \gtrsim \int |u|^2 d x \quad \text{(observability)}$$
  hold uniformly for all eigenfunctions $u$ of the Laplacian. Sufficient
conditions are derived based on the integrability and regularity of $\mu$,
while necessary conditions are formulated in terms of the dimension of the
support of the measure. These results generalize classical theorems of Zygmund
and Bourgain--Rudnick to higher dimensions. Applications include results in the
spirit of Cantor--Lebesgue theorems, constraints on quantum limits, and control
theory for the Schr\"odinger equation. Our approach combines several tools: the
cluster structure of lattice points on spheres; decoupling estimates; and the
construction of eigenfunctions exhibiting strong concentration or vanishing
behavior, tailored respectively to the trace and observability inequalities.

</details>


### [40] [Sharp Boundary Growth Rate Estimate of the Singular Equation $-Δ u=u^{-γ}$ in a Critical Cone](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16319)
*Leyun Wu,Chilin Zhang*

Abstract: For $\gamma>0$, we study the sharp boundary growth rate estimate of solutions

\begin{equation*}
  -\Delta u=u^{-\gamma} \end{equation*} in a critical $C^{1,1}$ epigraphical
cone $Cone_{\Sigma}$.
  We show that the growth rate estimate exhibits fundamentally different
behaviors in the following three cases: $1<\gamma<2$, $\gamma=2$, and
$\gamma>2$. Moreover, we obtain the sharp growth rate estimate near the origin
for $\gamma>1$. As a consequence, we show that when $Cone_{\Sigma}$ is a
$C^{1,1}$ epigraphical cone, the additional solvability condition in
\cite[Theorem 1.3]{GuLiZh25} is both sufficient and necessary to achieve the
growth rate therein, thereby resolving the main open question left in that
paper. With the growth rate estimate, we also derive the optimal modulus of
continuity for solutions via the interior Schauder estimate.
  Our approach is to control the values of a solution $U(x)$ in the region
$\Omega=Cone_{\Sigma}\cap B_{1}$ by introducing a sequence of reference points
$p_{k}=\frac{16^{1-k}}{2}\vec{e_{n}}$. From the Green function representation
of $U(x)$, we derive a discrete integral equation for the sequence
$a_{k}=16^{k\phi}U(p_{k})$. Such a computation converts the original PDE
problem into a recursion for a discrete integral equation, which can be
effectively analyzed using basic ODE methods.

### [43] [The fully nonlinear Loewner-Nirenberg problem: Liouville theorems and counterexamples to local boundary estimates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16383)
*Jonah A. J. Duncan,Luc Nguyen*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文完整分类了保角不变方程的正粘性解，发现当μ_Γ^+ > 1时唯一解是双曲解，当μ_Γ^+ ≤ 1时存在单参数解族，并给出了Loewner-Nirenberg问题边界估计的反例


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究保角不变方程f(λ(-A_w)) = 1/2在上半空间中的正粘性解分类问题，特别是Loewner-Nirenberg问题的解结构，以及理解不同参数条件下解的存在性和唯一性

Method: 采用移动球面法的新颖应用，建立边界附近的新估计和正则性理论，结合精细的常微分方程分析技术来分类解的结构

Result: 当μ_Γ^+ > 1时，双曲解w^(0)(x) = x_n是唯一解；当μ_Γ^+ ≤ 1时，解集包含单调递增的单参数解族{w^(a)(x_n)}_{a≥0}，其中双曲解是最小解。所有解都只依赖于x_n变量

Conclusion: 完成了保角不变方程正粘性解的完整分类，揭示了参数μ_Γ^+在决定解结构中的关键作用，并构造了当μ_Γ^+ ≤ 1时完全非线性Loewner-Nirenberg问题局部边界C^0估计的反例

Abstract: In this paper we give a complete classification of positive viscosity
solutions $w$ to conformally invariant equations of the form
  \begin{align}\label{ab}\tag{$*$}
  \begin{cases}
  f(\lambda(-A_w)) = \frac{1}{2}, \quad \lambda(-A_w)\in\Gamma & \text{in
}\mathbb{R}_+^n \newline
  w = 0 & \text{on }\partial\mathbb{R}_+^n,
  \end{cases}
  \end{align}
  where $A_w$ is the Schouten tensor of the metric $g_w = w^{-2}|dx|^2$,
$\Gamma\subset\mathbb{R}^n$ is a symmetric convex cone and $f$ is an associated
defining function satisfying standard assumptions. Solutions to \eqref{ab}
yield metrics $g_w$ of negative curvature-type which are locally complete near
$\partial\mathbb{R}_+^n$. In particular, when $(f,\Gamma) =
(\sigma_1,\Gamma_1^+)$, \eqref{ab} is the Loewner-Nirenberg problem in the
upper half-space.
  More precisely, let $\mu_\Gamma^+$ denote the unique constant satisfying
$(-\mu_\Gamma^+, 1,\dots,1)\in\partial\Gamma$. We show that when $\mu_\Gamma^+
>1$ (e.g. when $\Gamma = \Gamma_k^+$ for $k<\frac{n}{2}$), the hyperbolic
solution $w^{(0)}(x) := x_n$ is the unique solution to \eqref{ab}. More
surprisingly, we show that when $\mu_\Gamma^+ \leq 1$ (e.g. when $\Gamma =
\Gamma_k^+$ for $k\geq \frac{n}{2}$), the solution set consists of a
monotonically increasing one-parameter family $\{w^{(a)}(x_n)\}_{a\geq 0}$, of
which the hyperbolic solution $w^{(0)}$ is the minimal solution. In either
case, solutions of \eqref{ab} are functions of $x_n$. Our proof involves a
novel application of the method of moving spheres for which we must establish
new estimates and regularity near $\partial\mathbb{R}_+^n$, followed by a
delicate ODE analysis. As an application, we give counterexamples to local
boundary $C^0$ estimates on solutions to the fully nonlinear Loewner-Nirenberg
problem when $\mu_\Gamma^+ \leq 1$.

semilinear heat equation on the Heisenberg group involving a mixed local and
nonlocal nonlinearity. The characteristic features of such equations, arising
from the interplay between the geometric structure of the Heisenberg group and
the combined nonlinearity, are analyzed in detail. The need to distinguish
between subcritical and supercritical regimes is identified and justified
through rigorous analysis. On the basis of the study, the author suggests
precise conditions under which local-in-time mild solutions exist uniquely for
regular, nonnegative initial data. It is proved that global existence holds
under appropriate growth restrictions on the nonlinear terms. To complement
these results, it is shown, by employing the capacity method, that solutions
cannot exist globally in time when the nonlinearity exceeds a critical
threshold. As a result, the Fujita exponent is formulated and identified as the
dividing line between global existence and finite-time blow-up. In addition,
lifespan estimates were obtained in the supercritical regime, providing insight
into how the size of the initial data influences the time of blow-up.

</details>

regular mobility functions. Next, under weaker assumptions on the mobility
functions, we show the existence of a weak solution that exhibits the
propagation of uniform-in-time regularity and satisfies the instantaneous
separation property. Lastly, we consider the long-time behavior and prove that
the unique weak solution converges to a solution of the stationary bulk-surface
Cahn--Hilliard equation. Our approach for the uniqueness proof relies on a new
well-posedness and regularity theory for a bulk-surface elliptic system with
non-constant coefficients, which may be of independent interest.

find small losses of regularity in both the scalar field and the potential.

### [58] [On the intersection of Cantor set with the unit circle and some sequences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16510)
*Kan Jiang,Derong Kong,Wenxia Li,Zhiqiang Wang*

Main category: math.CA

TL;DR: 本文研究了自相似集合K_λ的笛卡尔积与单位圆的交集问题，证明了当λ∈(0, 2-√3]时交集是平凡的，而当λ较大时交集可以具有连续统的基数，并建立了基于勒让德符号的二分法来刻画这类交集的算术约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文的动机是研究自相似集合（康托集）的笛卡尔积与非线性曲线（特别是单位圆）的交集性质。这个问题由Yu在2023年提出，作者旨在给出该问题的否定答案，并建立更一般的理论框架来分析此类几何与算术相结合的问题。

Method: 作者采用了多种数学工具：1）分析自相似集合K_λ的结构性质；2）运用数论方法，特别是二次互反律和勒让德符号；3）建立基于数字集合的勒让德符号的二分法；4）通过构造特定的序列{λ_n}来证明边界值2-√3的尖锐性；5）将方法推广到一般的非线性曲线。

Result: 主要结果包括：1）当λ∈(0, 2-√3]时，单位圆与K_λ×K_λ的交集是平凡的，仅包含两点{(0,1), (1,0)}；2）当λ∈[0.330384, 1/2)时，交集是非平凡的；3）当λ∈[0.407493, 1/2)时，交集具有连续统的基数；4）边界值2-√3是尖锐的；5）建立了基于勒让德符号的二分法来刻画康托集与某些序列的交集。

Conclusion: 本文完全解决了Yu（2023）提出的问题，给出了否定答案，并建立了更深入的理论。通过引入数论工具，特别是勒让德符号，揭示了支配此类交集的基本算术约束。这些方法不仅适用于单位圆，还可以推广到许多其他非线性曲线，为几何与数论的交叉研究提供了新的视角和工具。

Abstract: For $\lambda\in(0,1/2)$ let $K_\lambda$ be the self-similar set in
$\mathbb{R}$ generated by the iterated function system $\{f_0(x)=\lambda x,
f_1(x)=\lambda x+1-\lambda \}$. In this paper, we investigate the intersection
of the unit circle $\mathbb{S} \subset \mathbb{R}^2$ with the Cartesian product
$K_{\lambda} \times K_{\lambda}$. We prove that for $\lambda \in(0, 2 -
\sqrt{3}]$, the intersection is trivial, i.e., \[ \mathbb{S} \cap (K_{\lambda}
\times K_{\lambda}) = \{(0,1), (1,0)\}. \] If $\lambda\in [0.330384,1/2)$, then
the intersection $\mathbb{S} \cap (K_{\lambda} \times K_{\lambda})$ is
non-trivial. In particular, if $\lambda\in [0.407493 , 1/2)$ the intersection
$\mathbb{S} \cap (K_{\lambda} \times K_{\lambda})$ is of cardinality continuum.
Furthermore, the bound $2 - \sqrt{3}$ is sharp: there exists a sequence
$\{\lambda_n\}_{n \in \mathbb{N}}$ with $\lambda_n \searrow 2 - \sqrt{3}$ such
that $\mathbb{S} \cap (K_{\lambda_n} \times K_{\lambda_n})$ is non-trivial for
all $n\in\mathbb{N}$. This result provides a negative answer to a problem posed
by Yu (2023). Our methods extend beyond the unit circle and remain effective
for many nonlinear curves. By employing tools from number theory, including the
quadratic reciprocity law, we analyze the intersection of Cantor sets with some
sequences. A dichotomy is established in terms of the Legendre symbol
associated with the digit set, revealing a fundamental arithmetic constraint
governing such intersections.

</details>

### [59] [The dependency digraph for irreducible finite-range random walk in free groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.15902)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了证明树上不可约等变有限范围随机游走通过概率的任意阶渐近展开，需要深入研究相关数学对象的解析和几何性质，特别是自由群上随机游走的依赖结构。

Method: 引入"淹没洞穴树"(flooded cavern tree)的定义作为主要工具，用于精确分析给定不可约有限范围随机游走在自由群上的依赖有向图的结构和性质。

Result: 通过淹没洞穴树的概念，成功分析了[Che25b]中引入对象的解析和几何性质，为理解自由群上随机游走的依赖关系提供了新的几何视角。

Conclusion: 该研究为三部曲的整体目标奠定了理论基础，通过几何方法深化了对树上随机游走通过概率渐近行为的理解，淹没洞穴树概念为分析复杂依赖结构提供了有效工具。

Abstract: This article is one of a triptych composed with [Che25a] and [Che25b], that
aims at proving an asymptotic expansion to any order of the passage probability
of an irreducible equivariant finite range random walk on a tree. In this text
we study the analytic and geometric properties of the objects introduced in
[Che25b]. To do so we introduce the definition of a ''flooded cavern tree''

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 建立聚合物测度族$M^{\theta}_{[s,t]}$的条件高斯乘性混沌结构，以随机测度$M^{\theta}_{[s,t]}$为参考测度构造路径空间GMC，并证明所得随机测度在分布意义下等于$M^{\theta+a}_{[s,t]}$。

Result: 成功证明了聚合物测度族具有条件GMC结构，建立了路径空间GMC与参数平移聚合物测度的等价性关系，并据此证明了聚合物测度和SHF对一般非负函数测试时几乎必然严格为正，以及SHF在$\theta\to\infty$时收敛到0。

Conclusion: 聚合物测度族$M^{\theta}_{[s,t]}$具有条件高斯乘性混沌结构，这一发现不仅揭示了其深层数学性质，还为证明聚合物测度的严格正性和随机热流的渐近行为提供了有力工具。

Abstract: We establish that the family of polymer measures $M^{\theta}_{[s,t]}$

structure. Namely, taking the random measure $M^{\theta}_{[s,t]}$ as the
reference measure, we construct the path-space GMC with noise strength $a > 0$
and prove that the resulting random measure is equal in law to
$M^{\theta+a}_{[s,t]}$. As two applications, we prove that the polymer measure
and SHF tested against general nonnegative functions are almost surely strictly
positive and that the SHF converges to $0$ as $\theta\to\infty$.

### [61] [The noisy voter model with general initial conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16188)
*Patrizio Caddeo,Eyal Lubetzky*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文研究了在有界度图上的噪声投票模型，证明了对于所有初始状态都存在明确的cutoff现象，并确认了交替初始条件在一维Ising模型中是渐近最快的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 之前的研究只针对二元情况(q=2)和最坏情况初始状态证明了cutoff现象，而对于更快的初始条件和更一般的q状态情况缺乏理论分析。此外，需要验证关于交替初始状态在所有噪声参数下都是最优的猜想。

Method: 通过分析噪声投票模型的自相关函数，建立了cutoff时间与初始状态自相关的明确函数关系。利用这一理论框架来分析不同图结构和不同状态数下的最优初始条件。

Result: 证明了对于任意有界度图和所有θ、q值以及初始状态，噪声投票模型都表现出cutoff现象。确认了一维环上二元情况下交替初始条件对所有θ值都是渐近最快的。同时证明了高维情况下棋盘模式初始条件和一维多状态情况下彩虹初始条件的最优性。

Conclusion: 该研究完整解决了噪声投票模型的cutoff现象问题，建立了通用的理论框架，并验证了之前关于最优初始条件的重要猜想，为理解马尔可夫链混合时间提供了重要理论贡献。

Abstract: We study the noisy voter model with $q\geq 2$ states and noise probability
$\theta$ on arbitrary bounded-degree $n$-vertex graphs $G$ with subexponential
growth of balls (e.g., finite subsets of $\mathbb{Z}^d$). Cox, Peres and Steif
(2016) showed for the binary case $q=2$ (and a wider class of chains) that,
when starting from a worst-case initial state, this Markov chain has total
variation cutoff at $t_n=\frac1{2\theta}\log n$. The second author and Sly
(2021) analyzed faster initial conditions for Glauber dynamics for the 1D Ising
model, which is the noisy voter for $q=2$ and $G=\mathbb{Z}/n\mathbb{Z}$. They
showed that the ``alternating'' initial state is the fastest one if $\theta\geq
\frac23$, and conjectured that this holds for all values of the noise $\theta$.
  Here we show that for every graph $G$ as above and all $\theta,q$ and initial
states $x_0$, the noisy voter model exhibits cutoff at an explicit function of
the autocorrelation of the model started at $x_0$. Consequently, for
$G=\mathbb{Z}/n\mathbb{Z}$ and $q=2$ (Glauber dynamics for the 1D Ising model),
we confirm the conjecture of [LS21] that the alternating initial condition is
asymptotically fastest for all $\theta$. Analogous results hold in
$\mathbb{Z}_n^d$ for $q=2$ and all $d\geq 1$ (``checkerboard'' initial
conditions are fastest) as well as for $d=1$ and all $q\geq 2$ (``rainbow''
initial conditions are fastest).

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We introduce a dynamic random hypergraph model constructed from a bipartite
graph. In this model, both vertex sets of the bipartite graph are generated by
marked Poisson point processes. Vertices of both vertex sets are equipped with
marks representing their weight that influence their connection radii.
Additionally, we also assign the vertices of the first vertex set a birth-death
process with exponential lifetimes and the vertices of the second vertex set a
time instant representing the occurrence of the corresponding vertices.
Connections between vertices are established based on the marks and the
birth-death processes, leading to a weighted dynamic hypergraph model featuring
power-law degree distributions. We analyze the edge-count process in two
distinct regimes. In the case of finite fourth moments, we establish a
functional central limit theorem for the normalized edge count, showing
convergence to a Gaussian AR(2)-type process as the observation window grows.
In the challenging case of the heavy-tailed regime with infinite variance, we
prove convergence to a novel stable process that is not L\'evy and not even
Markov.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 证明在调制链的平稳分布下，投票定理的一般形式仍然成立；2) 基于多元拉格朗日反演方法，推导风险过程各种击中时间的分布结果；3) 分别针对初始盈余为零和任意初始盈余的情况建立理论框架。

Abstract: In this paper, we study finite-time ruin probabilities for the compound
Markov binomial risk model - a discrete-time model where claim sizes are
modulated by a finite-state ergodic Markov chain. In the classic
(non-modulated) case, the risk process has interchangeable increments and
consequently, its finite-time ruin probability can be obtained in terms of
Tak\'acs' famous Ballot Theorem results. Unfortunately, due to the dependency
of our process on the state(s) of the modulating chain these do not necessarily
extend to the modulated setting. We show that a general form of the Ballot
Theorem remains valid under the stationary distribution of the modulating
chain, yielding a Tak\'acs-type expression for the finite-time ruin probability
which holds only when the initial surplus is equal to zero. For the case of
arbitrary initial surplus, we develop an approach based on multivariate
Lagrangian inversion, from which we derive distributional results for various
hitting times of the risk process, including a Seal-type formula for the
finite-time ruin probability.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用Lévy过程理论，特别是树数量t_n和森林数量f_n之间的Lévy过程关系，应用Hawkes和Jenkins的极限理论来分析随机森林的渐近行为。方法还扩展到次指数加权整数分割的枚举问题。

Abstract: Inspired by Stufler's recent probabilistic proof of Otter's asymptotic number
of unlabeled trees, we revisit work of Palmer and Schwenk, and study unlabeled
forests from a probabilistic point of view. We show that the number of trees in
a random forest converges, with all of its moments, to a shifted compound
Poisson. We also find the asymptotic proportion of forests that are trees. The
key fact is that the number of trees $t_n$ and forests $f_n$ are related by a
L\'evy process. As such, the results by Palmer and Schwenk follow by an earlier
and far-reaching limit theory by Hawkes and Jenkins. We also show how this
limit theory implies results by Schwenk and by Meir and Moon, related to
degrees in large random trees. Our arguments apply, more generally, to the
enumeration of sub-exponentially weighted integer partitions, or, in fact, any
setting where the underlying L\'evy process follows the one big jump principle.

### [68] [Particle systems and the supercooled Stefan problem with non-integrable initial data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16703)

Method: 构建正实轴上的无限粒子系统，粒子按泊松点过程初始化，遵循布朗运动直到撞击动态障碍；当障碍被撞击时会增加高度，允许连续跳跃瞬间发生；通过标度极限分析建立与过冷Stefan问题的数学联系。

Result: 在特定条件下，标度极限给出了过冷Stefan问题及其自由边界的表示；确定了障碍函数的精确渐近极限和收敛速率，解决了arXiv:1112.6257中的一个猜想；在临界情况下（跳跃大小匹配泊松过程密度且Stefan问题发生瞬时爆炸），恢复了与arXiv:1705.10017相同的标度极限结果。

Conclusion: 通过粒子系统的随机表示成功建立了过冷Stefan问题的新数学框架，不仅解决了已有猜想，还扩展了对非L¹初始数据情况的理解，在临界参数下验证了理论的一致性。

Abstract: We consider an infinite system of particles on the positive real line,
initiated from a Poisson point process, which move according to Brownian motion
up until the hitting time of a barrier. The barrier increases when it is hit,
allowing for the possibility of sequences of successive jumps to occur
instantaneously. Under certain conditions, the scaling limit gives a
representation for the supercooled Stefan problem and its free boundary. This
allows us to give a precise asymptotic limit for the barrier and determine the
rate of convergence, resolving a conjecture of arXiv:1112.6257. From this
representation, we also investigate properties of the supercooled Stefan
problem for initial data not in $L^1(\mathbb{R}^+)$. In a critical case, where
the jump size matches the density of the Poisson process and the Stefan problem
has an instantaneous explosion, we instead recover the same scaling limit
result as in arXiv:1705.10017.

</details>

### [69] [Point counts, automorphisms, and gonalities of Shimura curves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.15992)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该点数计算算法在解决算术问题方面具有实用价值，不仅能够找到具有极值点数性质的曲线，还能用于研究曲线的自同构群结构和几何性质的分类问题。

Abstract: We implement an algorithm to compute the number of points over finite fields

in this field is the well-known odd covering problem. In this paper, we
investigate a variant of that problem, where one odd integer is permitted to

### [71] [The structure of the double discriminant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16138)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 证明了当k=0时，双判别式DD_{n,k}确实可以表示为一个平方、一个立方和可能的线性单项式的乘积；同时研究了因式分解中通常较大且光滑的整数常数的性质

Conclusion: 双判别式DD_{n,k}具有特定的因式分解结构，在k=0时得到了完整证明，为van der Waerden-Bhargava定理的理论基础提供了更深入的代数几何理解

Abstract: For a polynomial $f(x) = \sum_{i=0}^n a_i x^i$, we study the double
discriminant $DD_{n,k} = \operatorname{disc}_{a_k} \operatorname{disc}_x f(x)$,
which appears in the proof of the van der Waerden--Bhargava theorem. We
conjecture that $DD_{n,k}$ is the product of a square, a cube, and possibly a
linear monomial and we prove this when $k=0$. We also investigate the
(typically large and smooth) outlying integer constant in the factorization of
$DD_{n,k}$.

*David Savitt*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为有天赋的高中生教授Newman关于eta商函数模性的定理，需要一个避免复杂技术（如Dedekind和）的初等证明方法。

Method: 关键观察是虽然Γ₁(N)不能由其上三角和下三角子群生成，但可以由这些子群连同任意同余子群一起生成。利用eta函数乘子系统的一个简单恒等式来建立相对于某个同余子群的模性。

Result: 成功给出了Newman定理的一个初等证明，该证明适合高中生理解，避免了Dedekind和等高深技术，仅使用群论结构的基本性质。

Conclusion: 通过巧妙的群论观察和eta函数乘子系统的简单恒等式，可以给出Newman关于eta商函数模性定理的初等证明，这为数学教育提供了一个更易理解的方法。

Abstract: Let eta(z) be the Dedekind eta function. Newman studied the modularity of
eta-quotients, giving necessary and sufficient conditions for a function of the
form \prod_{0 < m | N} eta(mz)^{r_m} to be a (weakly) holomorphic modular form
of level N. We explain a proof of Newman's theorem, developed while teaching a
class for talented high school students at Canada/USA Mathcamp. The key
observation is that although Gamma_1(N) is not generated by its upper
triangular and lower triangular subgroups, it is generated by those subgroups
together with any congruence subgroup. Modularity with respect to some
congruence subgroup is established using one simple identity involving the
multiplier system of eta(z), whose proof is elementary in the sense that it
avoids the use of Dedekind sums.

### [73] [The SOS Rank of Biquadratic Forms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16399)
*Liqun Qi,Chunfeng Cui,Yi Xu*

Main category: math.NT

TL;DR: 本文研究了多元二次型的平方和表示问题，将m×2正半定双二次型的平方和秩问题转化为退化三部四次型的研究，并证明了相关的结构性质和判别式表示结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Calderón在1973年证明了m×2正半定双二次型可以表示为3m(m+1)/2个二次型的平方和，最近作者改进了m=2的情况。对于m≥3的情况，平方和秩问题仍待进一步探索，这是本文的研究动机。

Method: 通过将具有非平凡零点的m×n正半定双二次型表示为(m-1)×(n-1)×1退化三部四次型，将m×2正定双二次型分解为一个二次型的平方与一个(m-1)×1×1退化三部四次型的和，从而将原问题转化为研究退化三部四次型的平方和秩问题。

Result: 证明了m×2正半定双二次型的平方和秩问题可以归结为(m-1)×1×1退化三部四次型的平方和秩问题。同时证明了(m-1)×1×1退化三部四次型至少有两个非平凡零点，以及2×1×1退化三部四次型的判别式可以表示为三个三次型的平方和。

Conclusion: 通过引入退化三部四次型的概念和方法，成功地将复杂的m×2双二次型平方和秩问题转化为更简单的低维问题，为进一步解决这类问题提供了新的理论框架和技术路径。

Abstract: In 1973, Calder\'{o}n proved that an $m \times 2$ positive semidefinite (psd)
biquadratic form can always be expressed as the sum of squares (sos) of
${3m(m+1) \over 2}$ quadratic forms. Very recently, by applying Hilbert's
theorem, we proved that a $2 \times 2$ psd biquadratic form can always be
expressed as the sum of squares of three quadratic forms. This improved
Calder\'{o}n's result for $m=2$, and left the sos rank problem of $m \times 2$
biquadratic forms for $m \ge 3$ to further exploration. In this paper, we show
that an $m \times n$ psd biquadratic form with a nontrivial zero {can} be
expressed as an $(m-1) \times (n-1) \times 1$ degenerated tripartite quartic
form. Furthermore, we show that an $m \times 2$ positive definite (pd)
biquadratic form can be expressed as the sum of a square of a quadratic form,
and an $(m-1) \times 1 \times 1$ degenerated tripartite quartic form. Thus, the
sos rank problem of $m \times 2$ psd biquadratic forms is reduced to the sos
rank problem of an $(m-1) \times 1 \times 1$ degenerated tripartite quartic
forms. We then show that an $(m-1) \times 1 \times 1$ degenerated tripartite
quartic form has at least two nontrivial zeros, and the discriminent of a $2
\times 1 \times 1$ degenerated tripartite quartic form can be expressed as the
sum of the square of three cubic forms.

</details>


### [74] [Hausdorff dimension of the graph of the error-sum function of continued fractions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16536)
*Min Woong Ahn*

Main category: math.NT

TL;DR: 本文研究无权重误差和函数的Hausdorff维数，证明其图的Hausdorff维数恰好为1，并重新推导相对误差和函数图的Hausdorff维数上界为3/2


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究连分数收敛逼近中误差累积函数的几何性质，特别是其图形的分形维数特征，这在数论和几何测度论的交叉领域具有重要理论意义

Method: 采用数论方法，包括Möbius反演、互质收敛分母求和技术，以及通过连分数递推关系推导精确上界的分析技术

Result: 证明了无权重误差和函数E(x)图的Hausdorff维数恰好等于1，并作为补充结果重新推导了相对误差和函数P(x)图的Hausdorff维数上界为3/2

Conclusion: 通过严格的数论分析确定了连分数误差和函数的精确分形维数，为理解连分数逼近的几何性质提供了新的理论基础

Abstract: We study the unweighted error-sum function $\mathcal{E}(x) \coloneqq \sum_{n
\geq 0} ( x- p_n(x)/q_n(x) )$, where $p_n(x)/q_n(x)$ is the $n$th convergent of
the continued fraction expansion of $x \in \mathbb{R}$. We prove that the
Hausdorff dimension of the graph of $\mathcal{E}$ is exactly $1$. Our proof is
number-theoretic in nature and involves M\"obius inversion, summation over
coprime convergent denominators, and precise upper bounds derived via continued
fraction recurrence relations. As a supplementary result, we rederive the known
upper bound of $3/2$ for the Hausdorff dimension of the graph of the relative
error-sum function $P(x) \coloneqq \sum_{n \geq 0} (q_n(x)x-p_n(x))$.

### [79] [Periodic Hypersurfaces and Lee-Yang Polynomials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16029)
*Lior Alon,Mario Kummer*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 该论文证明了一个关于$\mathbb{Z}^n$-周期$C^{1+\epsilon}$-超曲面$\Sigma$为代数曲面的傅里叶判据，即存在多项式$p$使得$\Sigma=\{x\in\mathbb{R}^n : p(e^{2\pi i x_1},\dots,e^{2\pi i x_n})=0\}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立周期超曲面是否为代数曲面的判定准则，这在数学分析和代数几何的交叉领域具有重要意义，特别是在理解周期结构的代数性质方面。

Method: 通过构造周期测度$m_{\ell}$和引入"灯塔"概念，利用傅里叶分析技术建立判据。具体地，对每个方向$\ell\in\mathbb{R}^n$定义周期测度$dm_{\ell}(x)=|\langle\ell,\hat n(x)\rangle|\,d\sigma(x)$，然后要求存在Q-线性无关的$\ell$和闭锥$C$，使得傅里叶系数$\widehat{m}_{\ell}(k)$在$k\notin C\cup(-C)$时为零。

Result: 证明了在满足"灯塔"条件下，超曲面$\Sigma$确实可以表示为$\Sigma(p)$的形式，并且经过适当的单项式变换后，多项式$p$可以取为Lee-Yang多项式。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了周期超曲面代数性的傅里叶判据，证明依赖于最近关于一维傅里叶准晶体的刻画结果，为理解周期几何结构的代数性质提供了新的分析工具。

Abstract: We prove a Fourier criterion for a $\mathbb{Z}^n$-periodic
$C^{1+\epsilon}$-hypersurface $\Sigma\subset\mathbb{R}^n$ to be algebraic in
the sense that $\Sigma=\Sigma(p):=\{x\in\mathbb{R}^n : p(e^{2\pi i
x_1},\dots,e^{2\pi i x_n})=0\}$ for some polynomial $p$. More precisely, each
direction $\ell\in\mathbb{R}^n$ defines a periodic measure $m_{\ell}$ on
$\Sigma$ by $dm_{\ell}(x)=|\langle\ell,\hat n(x)\rangle|\,d\sigma(x)$, with
$\hat n(x)$ the unit normal to $\Sigma$ and $\sigma$ its $n-1$ dimensional
surface measure. Our Fourier criterion for $\Sigma$ is that there exists
$\ell\in\mathbb{R}^n$ with Q-linearly independent entries and a closed cone
$C\subset\mathbb{R}^n$ for which $\langle\ell,v\rangle>0$ for all nonzero $v\in
C$, such that for $k\in\mathbb{Z}^n$ we have
$\widehat{m}_{\ell}(k)=\int_{\Sigma/\mathbb{Z}^n}e^{2\pi i\langle
k,x\rangle}\,dm_{\ell}(x)=0$ for every $k\notin C\cup(-C)$. Using Meyers
terminology this says $(m_{\ell},C)$ is a "lighthouse". Under this hypothesis
one shows $\Sigma=\Sigma(p)$, and after a suitable monomial change $p$ can be
taken as a Lee-Yang polynomial. The proof relies on a recent characterization
of all one-dimensional Fourier quasicrystals.

</details>

### [90] [The ranks of twists of an elliptic curve in characteristic $3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16785)

### [91] [Genus Zero Kashiwara-Vergne Solutions from Braids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16243)
*Zsuzsanna Dancso,Iva Halacheva,Guillaume Laplante-Anfossi,Marcy Robertson,Chandan Singh*

Main category: math.AT

TL;DR: 本文使用moperad理论重新解释了Alekseev-Enriquez-Torossian构造的Kashiwara-Vergne解，建立了带冻结股的加括号辫子moperad与弦图moperad之间的同构关系，并研究了相关的群作用和因式分解条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的Kashiwara-Vergne问题解法缺乏统一的代数框架，需要使用moperad理论来重新解释和理解Alekseev-Enriquez-Torossian构造，从而揭示KV解与各种代数结构之间的深层联系。

Method: 采用moperad（作为operad上右模范畴中的monoid）的语言框架，研究带冻结股的加括号辫子moperad与弦图moperad之间的同构关系，分析Grothendieck-Teichmüller模群的作用，并构造从KV解到自由李代数切向自同构moperad的态射。

Result: 证明了带冻结股的加括号辫子moperad与弦图moperad之间的任何同构都会产生一族零亏格KV解，这些解由单个经典KV解通过operad方式生成；展示了Grothendieck-Teichmüller模群在其上的作用如何与KV对称群的作用相互缠绕；建立了对称KV解与相应态射之间的对应关系。

Conclusion: 成功建立了moperad理论框架下的KV问题新解释，揭示了KV解与辫子、弦图、自由李代数等代数结构之间的本质联系，特别是证明了态射通过弦图moperad因式分解当且仅当相关的KV结合子是Drinfeld结合子，为理解KV问题提供了新的代数几何视角。

Abstract: Using the language of moperads-monoids in the category of right modules over
an operad-we reinterpret the Alekseev-Enriquez-Torossian construction of
Kashiwara-Vergne (KV) solutions from associators. We show that any isomorphism
between the moperad of parenthesized braids with a frozen strand and the
moperad of chord diagrams gives rise to a family of genus zero KV solutions
operadically generated by a single classical KV solution. We show that the
Grothendieck-Teichm\"uller module groups act on the latter, intertwining the
actions of the KV symmetry groups. In the other direction, we show that any
symmetric KV solution gives rise to a morphism from the moperad of
parenthesized braids with a frozen strand to the moperad of tangential
automorphisms of free Lie algebras. This morphism factors through the moperad
of chord diagrams if and only if the associated KV associator is a Drinfeld
associator.

</details>

*Anthony Agwu*

Main category: math.CT

TL;DR: 本文研究了在偏组合代数A上的装配范畴中内部定义的群胚范畴Grpd(Asm(A))，展示了其π-部落结构，证明了该范畴是类型论的模型，并构造了分割群胚装配的子范畴pGrpd(Asm(A))，建立了其与可实现性拓扑的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过展示Grpd(Asm(A))上的π-部落结构来证明其为类型论模型；构造带约简的W-类型和装配的一元对象分类器；利用W-类型建立模型结构；构造分割群胚装配的完整子范畴pGrpd(Asm(A))并研究其性质。

Abstract: As a discretization of the Hodge Laplacian, the combinatorial Laplacian of

matrix-tree theorem for complex pairs, which generalizes both the matrix-tree
theorem for simplicial complexes proved by Duval, Klivans, and Martin (2009)
and the result for Dirichlet eigenvalues of graph pairs by Chung (1996).
Furthermore, we derive several lower bounds for the spectral gaps of complex

homology. Our results demonstrate that the combinatorial Laplacians for complex
pairs are closely related to relative homology.

the central graph C(G) of G is obtained from S(G) after joining all
non-adjacent vertices of G.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析平面图的结构性质和避免C₃∪C₅子图的约束条件，运用图论技巧和组合分析方法来确定极值函数的精确值，并构造或刻画达到这一上界的极值图结构。

Abstract: The planar Tur\'an number of $H$, denoted by $ex_{\mathcal{P}}(n,H)$, is the
maximum number of edges in an $n$-vertex $H$-free planar graph. The planar
Tur\'an number of $k\geq 3$ vertex-disjoint union of cycles is the trivial
value $3n-6$. Let $C_{\ell}$ denote the cycle of length $\ell$ and
$C_{\ell}\cup C_t$ denote the union of disjoint cycles $C_{\ell}$ and $C_t$.
The planar Tur\'an number $ex_{\mathcal{P}}(n,H)$ is known if $H=C_{\ell}\cup
C_k$, where $\ell,k\in \{3,4\}$. In this paper, we determine the value
$ex_{\mathcal{P}}(n,C_3\cup C_5)=\lfloor\frac{8n-13}{3}\rfloor$ and
characterize the extremal graphs when $n$ is sufficiently large.

### [102] [$p$-th order generalized Fibonacci cubes and maximal cubes in Fibonacci $p$-cubes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16387)
*Michel Mollard*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了斐波那契立方体的推广——p阶斐波那契立方体，建立了其顶点与整数组合的联系，并研究了其枚举性质和立方多项式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典斐波那契立方体是超立方体的子图，由不含连续1的顶点诱导。为了进一步推广这一概念，需要研究更一般的p阶斐波那契立方体，即由不含p个连续1的字符串诱导的子图。

Method: 通过建立p阶斐波那契立方体顶点与部分在集合{1,2,...,p}中的整数组合之间的联系，利用组合数学方法研究其枚举性质。采用生成函数技术分析阶数、大小和立方多项式，并引入p-项式系数作为二项式系数的推广。

Result: 得到了p阶斐波那契立方体的阶数、大小和立方多项式的表达式及其生成函数。发现许多表达式与经典斐波那契立方体相似，但p-项式系数起到了二项式系数的作用。证明了斐波那契p-立方体中的最大诱导超立方体与(p+1)阶斐波那契立方体的顶点相关联。

Conclusion: 成功推广了斐波那契立方体的概念，建立了p阶斐波那契立方体与整数组合理论的深刻联系，并利用这种联系确定了斐波那契p-立方体的最大立方多项式，为图论和组合数学的交叉研究提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: The Fibonacci cube $\Gamma_n$ is the subgraph of the hypercube $Q_n$ induced
by vertices with no consecutive 1s. We study a one parameter generalization,
p-th order Fibonacci cubes $\Gamma^{(p)}_n$, which are subgraphs of $Q_n$
induced by strings without p consecutive 1s. We show the link between vertices
of $\Gamma^{(p)}_n$ and compositions of integers with parts in $\{1, 2, \ldots
, p\}$. Among other eumerative properties, we study the order, size and cube
polynomial of $\Gamma^{(p)}_n$ as well as their generating functions. Many of
the given expressions are similar to those for Fibonacci cubes, where the
$p$-nomial coefficients play the role of binomial coefficients. We also show
that maximal induced hypercubes in Fibonacci $p$-cubes $\Gamma^p_n$ , another
generalization of Fibonacci cubes, are connected to vertices of $(p + 1)$-th
order Fibonacci cubes. We use this link to determine the maximal cube
polynomial of Fibonacci $p$-cubes.

</details>

Abstract: The representation number of a graph is the minimum number of copies of each

corresponding to vertices $x$ and $y$ alternate if and only if $xy$ is an edge
in the graph. It is known that path graphs, circle graphs, and ladder graphs

graphs in the context of word-representability, which leads to an interesting
conjecture.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于帕累托最优决策原理，需要推断互反矩阵A的Perron特征向量w的效率，这需要通过研究与矩阵A和向量w相关的有向图的强连通性来实现。

Method: 通过分析互反矩阵的扩展性质，研究与扩展矩阵及其Perron特征向量相关的有向图结构，特别关注有向图中源点的存在性问题，并考虑一致矩阵的扰动情况。

Result: 证明了Furtado和Johnson提出的猜想：不存在互反矩阵的扩展，使得与该扩展及其Perron特征向量相关的有向图具有源点。对于n≥5的情况，描述了扰动参数x,y,z,a之间的关系，在这些关系下矩阵A总是具有高效的Perron特征向量。

Abstract: Let $A$ be a reciprocal matrix of order $n$ and $w$ be its Perron
eigenvector. To infer the efficiency of $w$ for $A$, based on the principle of
Pareto optimal decisions, we study the strong connectivity of a certain digraph
associated with $A$ and $w$. A reciprocal matrix $B$ of order $n+1$ is an
extension of $A$ if the matrix $A$ is obtained from $B$ by removing its last
row and column. We prove that there is no extension of a reciprocal matrix
whose digraph associated with the extension and its Perron eigenvector has a

Perron vector of a reciprocal matrix". As an application, considering $n\geq 5$

above the main diagonal, $x,y,z,a$, and the corresponding reciprocal entries,
in a way that there is a submatrix of size $2$ containing the four perturbed
entries and not containing a diagonal entry, we describe the relations among
$x,y,z,a$ with which $A$ always has efficient Perron eigenvector.

Abstract: The general position problem for graphs asks for the largest number of
vertices in a subset $S \subseteq V(G)$ of a graph $G$ such that for any $u,v
\in S$ and any shortest $u,v$-path $P$ we have $S \cap V(P) = \{ u,v\} $,
whereas the mutual visibility problem requires only that for any $u,v \in S$
there exists a shortest $u,v$-path with $S \cap V(P) = \{ u,v\} $. In the
mobile versions of these problems, robots must move through the network in
general position/mutual visibility such that every vertex is visited by a
robot. This paper solves some open problems from the literature. We quantify
the effect of adding the restriction that every robot can visit every vertex
(the so-called \emph{completely mobile} variants), prove a bound on both mobile
numbers in terms of the clique number, and find the mobile mutual visibility
number of line graphs of complete graphs, strong grids and Cartesian grids.

Magalhaes Jr.\ and Real (2024).
  Our central graph-theoretic tool is the use of tree-cut decompositions,
introduced by Wollan (2015) as a variation of tree decompositions that is based
on edge cuts instead of vertex separations. In particular, we give a new,
elementary proof for Kurkofka's result (2022) that every infinite graph has a
tree-cut decomposition of finite adhesion into its $\omega$-edge blocks. Along
the way, we also give a new, short proof for a classic result by Halin (1984)
on $K_{k,\kappa}$-subdivisions in $k$-connected graphs, making this paper
self-contained.

and the paths have associated Somos $4$ sequences which are essentially the
same. For the curves the link to Somos $4$ sequences is a classical result, via

transform.

*Zihao Jin,Sean Longbrake,Liana Yepremyan*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了Erdős-Simonovits猜想在边粘合操作下的保持性，证明了在一定对称条件下，如果两个图满足该猜想，则它们通过边粘合得到的图也满足该猜想，并证明了Zarankiewicz数在边粘合下具有阶的可加性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 1984年Erdős和Simonovits提出了一个关于二部图H的猜想：是否存在常数使得任何具有足够多边的图都包含足够多的H的副本。本文旨在研究这个猜想在图的边粘合操作下是否保持成立，以及探索Zarankiewicz数的性质。

Method: 采用图论中的边粘合技术，在温和的对称条件下分析猜想的保持性。主要方法包括：(1)研究两个满足Erdős-Simonovits猜想的图H1和H2通过固定边粘合后的性质；(2)分析将多个H的副本沿着H的子森林的同一标记副本粘合的情况；(3)利用符号二部图理论分析Zarankiewicz数的可加性。

Result: 证明了以下主要结果：(1)如果两个图H1和H2满足Erdős-Simonovits猜想，且沿固定边粘合产生唯一图，则结果图也满足该猜想；(2)如果H满足该猜想，将多个标记的H副本沿着H的子森林的同一标记副本粘合，结果图也满足该猜想；(3)对于符号二部图，Zarankiewicz数在保持边符号的边粘合下具有阶的可加性，即z(m,n,H) = Θ(z(m,n,H1) + z(m,n,H2))。

Conclusion: 边粘合操作在一定条件下保持Erdős-Simonovits猜想的成立性，这为理解该猜想提供了新的视角和工具。同时，Zarankiewicz数在边粘合下的可加性质揭示了极值图论中的深层结构性质，为进一步研究提供了理论基础。

Abstract: In 1984, Erd\H{o}s and Simonovits asked the following: given a bipartite
graph $H$, do there exist constants $0 \leq \alpha < 1$ and $\beta, C > 0$ such
that any graph $G$ on $n$ vertices and $pn^2\geq C n^{1+ \alpha}$ edges
contains at least $\beta n^{\mathrm{v}(H)} p^{\mathrm{e}(H)}$ copies of $H$?
  We show that edge-gluing preserves the satisfiability of this conjecture
under some mild symmetry conditions. Namely, if two graphs $H_1$ and $H_2$
satisfy this conjecture, and if furthermore, gluing them along a fixed edge
produces a unique graph then the resulting graph satisfies the conjecture as
well. We also show that if $H$ satisfies the conjecture then if we glue several
copies of (labeled) $H$ along the same labeled copy of a subforest of $H$ then
the resulting graph also satisfies the conjecture.
  We also show that Zarankiewicz numbers are additive in the order of magnitude
under gluing edges. Indeed, for a (signed) bipartite graph $H$ with parts
coloured $+$ and $-$, recall $z(m,n, H)$ is the maximum number of edges in a
signed bipartite graph $G$ with $+$ side being of size $m$ and $-$ side being
of size $n$ such that $G$ does not contain a copy of $H$ with $+$ side embedded
in the $+$ side of $G$. We show that for any two (signed) bipartite graphs
$H_1$ and $H_2$ if we glue them along an edge preserving the sign of the edge
then the resulting graph $H$ satisfies $z(m,n, H) = \Theta(z(m,n, H_1) + z(m,n,
H_2))$.

</details>

Method: 通过理论分析方法研究清醒环的性质，包括：1）分析环成为清醒环的充分条件；2）研究成为清醒环的必要条件；3）构造具体例子来说明该性质的行为特征；4）建立与其他已知环类的联系

Abstract: We introduce the class of sober rings and investigate it through several key

*Partha Kumbhakar,Varadharaj Ravi Srinivasan*

Main category: math.AC

TL;DR: 本文研究了微分域扩张的结构，证明了任何中间微分域都包含一个由Riccati方程解生成的子域或阿贝尔扩张，并应用此结果扩展了Goldman-Singer等人的经典结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究强正规微分域扩张中中间域的结构性质，特别是理解这些中间域如何通过Riccati方程的解或阿贝尔扩张来刻画，以便更好地理解线性微分方程的可解性问题。

Method: 对于微分域k的强正规扩张E，通过分析任意中间微分域K，构造一个中间域M，使其要么由k上Riccati微分方程的非代数解生成，要么使得k⁰M成为k⁰的阿贝尔扩张。

Result: 证明了中间微分域的结构定理：任何中间域都包含特定形式的子域。重新证明并扩展了Goldman和Singer的结果，研究了线性微分方程的d-可解性，并扩展了Rosenlicht关于代数微分方程解的代数相关性的结果。

Conclusion: 建立了强正规微分域扩张中中间域的完整结构刻画，为研究微分方程的可解性和解的性质提供了新的理论工具，并成功扩展了该领域的多个经典结果。

Abstract: Let $k$ be a differential field having an algebraically closed field of
constants, $E$ be a strongly normal extension of $k$, and $k^0$ be the
algebraic closure of $k$ in $E.$ We prove for any intermediate differential
field $k\subset K\subseteq E$ that there is an intermediate differential field
$k\subset M\subseteq K$ such that either $M$ is generated as a differential
field over $k$ by a nonalgebraic solution of a Riccati differential equation
over $k$ or $k^0M$ is an abelian extension of $k^0$. Using this result, we
reprove and extend certain results of Goldman and Singer and study
$d-$solvability of linear differential equations. We also extend a result of

differential equations.

### [121] [Hyperbolicity and Schwarz Lemmas in Calibrated Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16313)
*Kyle Broder,Anton Iliashenko,Jesse Madnick*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入KR $\phi$-度量（递减Finsler伪度量），定义$R_\phi$-双曲性和$\phi$-双曲性概念；推导Smith浸入（保形$\phi$-曲线）的Schwarz引理，引入$\phi$-截面曲率概念；利用Bochner公式进行分析。

Result: 证明了$R_\phi$-双曲性蕴含$\phi$-双曲性，但反之不成立；完全刻画了$\mathbb{R}^n$中常系数内Mobius刚性标定的$\phi$-双曲域；建立了标定流形中Smith浸入的Schwarz引理；计算了实、复、四元数双曲空间的KR $\phi$-度量。

Abstract: This paper has two main objectives. First, for an arbitrary calibrated
manifold $(X,\phi)$, we define notions of $R_\phi$-hyperbolicity and
$\phi$-hyperbolicity, which respectively generalize the notions of Kobayashi
and Brody hyperbolicity from complex geometry. To make sense of the former, we
introduce the "KR $\phi$-metric," a decreasing Finsler pseudo-metric that
specializes to the Kobayashi-Royden pseudo-metric in the Kahler case. We prove
that $R_\phi$-hyperbolicity implies $\phi$-hyperbolicity, and give examples
showing that the converse fails in general. Moreover, for constant-coefficient,
inner Mobius rigid calibrations $\phi$ in $\mathbb{R}^n$, we completely
characterize those domains that are $\phi$-hyperbolic.
  Second, we derive a Schwarz lemma for Smith immersions (a.k.a. conformal
$\phi$-curves) into an arbitrary calibrated manifold $(X, \phi)$, thereby
extending the Schwarz lemma for holomorphic curves into Kahler manifolds. The
relevant Bochner formula features the "$\phi$-sectional curvature," a new
notion that includes both the scalar and holomorphic sectional curvatures as
special cases. As an application, we prove that calibrated geometries with
$\phi$-sectional curvature bounded above by a negative constant are
$\phi$-hyperbolic, generalizing the corresponding result from complex geometry.
As another application, we calculate the KR $\phi$-metric of real, complex, and
quaternionic hyperbolic spaces equipped with their natural calibrations.

</details>

*Peter Hochs,Thijs de Kok*

Result: 成功将Roe的分割流形指标定理推广到非紧致超曲面的情况，得到了Roe代数K-理论中两个类之间的等式关系，这种等式关系是原有紧致情况下指标等式的自然推广

Abstract: Roe's partitioned manifold index theorem applies when a complete Riemannian
manifold $M$ is cut into two pieces along a compact hypersurface $N$. It states
that a version of the index of a Dirac operator on $M$ localized to $N$ equals
the index of the corresponding Dirac operator on $N$. This yields obstructions
to positive scalar curvature, and implies cobordism invariance of the index of
Dirac operators on compact manifolds. We generalize this result to cases where
$N$ may be noncompact, under assumptions on the way it is embedded into $M$.
This results in an equality between two classes in the $K$-theory of the Roe
algebra of $N$.

Conclusion: 建立了一系列关于嵌入毛细管边界MOTS的初始数据集边界刚性结果，从3维情况扩展到高维情况，为理解带边界时空的几何约束提供了重要的数学工具

Abstract: In this paper, we present the several rigidity results of initial data sets
with boundary when a marginally outer trap surface (MOTS) with capillary
boundary is embedded. First, we establish estimates for the area of a MOTS with
capillary boundary. Next, we prove a rigidity for 3-dimensional initial data

### [126] [Backwards uniqueness for Mean curvature flow with asymptotically conical singularities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16805)
*J. M. Daniels-Holgate,Or Hershkovits*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文证明了在特定条件下平均曲率流的后向唯一性：如果两个紧致超曲面的平均曲率流在第一奇异时间遇到相同的孤立、重数为一的渐近锥形奇异性，且在奇异时间两流重合，则它们在整个时间区间内都重合。这是首个不依赖自收缩或全局渐近锥形行为假设的几何流奇异性后向唯一性结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的几何流后向唯一性结果通常需要自收缩或全局渐近锥形行为的假设，这限制了其适用范围。本文旨在在更一般的条件下证明平均曲率流的后向唯一性，特别是针对具有孤立奇异性的情况，这对理解几何流的奇异性结构具有重要意义。

Method: 作者开发了新的全局工具来同时处理奇异性的核心、其渐近结构以及流的光滑部分。通过分析在第一奇异时间T具有相同终端状态的两个平均曲率流，利用孤立、重数为一、渐近锥形奇异性的特殊结构，建立了后向唯一性的证明框架。

Result: 成功证明了如果两个紧致超曲面的平均曲率流$M^1_t$和$M^2_t$在第一奇异时间T只遇到孤立、重数为一的渐近锥形奇异性，且$M^1_T=M^2_T$，则对于所有$t\in [0,T]$都有$M^1_t=M^2_t$。这是首个不依赖传统假设条件的几何流奇异性后向唯一性结果。

Conclusion: 本文建立了平均曲率流在奇异性情况下的后向唯一性理论，突破了以往需要自收缩或全局渐近锥形行为假设的限制。所开发的全局分析工具为研究几何流奇异性提供了新的方法，对几何分析和微分几何领域具有重要的理论价值。

Abstract: In this paper we demonstrate that if two mean curvature flows of compact
hypersurfaces $M^1_t$ and $M^2_t$ encounter only isolated, multiplicity one,
asymptotically conical singularities at the first singular time $T$, and if
$M^1_T=M^2_T$ then $M^1_t=M^2_t$ for every $t\in [0,T]$. This is seemingly the
first backwards uniqueness result for any geometric flow with singularities,
that assumes neither {self-shrinking} nor global asymptotically conical
{behaviour}. This necessitates the development of new global tools to deal with
both the core of the singularity, its asymptotic structure, and the smooth part
of the flows simultaneously.

</details>

Abstract: The D2 problem of C. T. C. Wall asks whether every finite cohomologically

quaternion group of order 32. We show that this CW-complex is homotopy

Motivation: 为给定的自由积分裂的纯对称外自同构提供几何生成元的证明，这是自由群外自同构理论中的一个重要问题

Method: 构造自由积外空间(Outer Space)的一个"好"子复形，利用几何方法而非代数方法来研究外自同构的结构

Result: 证明了给定自由积分裂的纯对称外自同构可以由两类基本外自同构生成：因子外自同构和相对于该分裂的Whitehead外自同构

Conclusion: 通过几何方法成功证明了自由积外自同构的生成元定理，为理解自由积的外自同构群结构提供了新的几何视角

Abstract: We construct a `nice' subcomplex of the Outer Space for a free product in
order to give a geometric proof that the pure symmetric outer automorphisms of
a given splitting of a free product are generated by factor outer automorphisms
and Whitehead outer automorphisms relative to the splittting.

</details>


### [135] [On the Isoperimetric functions of a class of Artin Groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16770)
*Arye Juhasz*

Main category: math.GR

TL;DR: 本文证明了特定Artin群(定义图中不包含标号为3的边)具有多项式(n^6)等周函数，并由此推导出偶Artin群的字问题是可解的


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Artin群的字问题可解性是群论中的重要问题。对于一般的Artin群，字问题的可解性仍然是开放问题。本文旨在证明特定类型的Artin群(定义图中不含标号为3的边)具有可解的字问题

Method: 使用相对扩展表示的小消去理论(small cancellation theory of relative extended presentations)来分析Artin群的几何和代数性质

Result: 证明了定义图中不包含标号为3的边的Artin群具有多项式度数为6的等周函数，即等周函数为O(n^6)。作为推论，证明了所有偶Artin群都有可解的字问题

Conclusion: 通过建立多项式等周函数，成功证明了一大类Artin群(包括所有偶Artin群)的字问题是可解的，这为理解Artin群的计算复杂性提供了重要进展

Abstract: We find a polynomial (n^6) isoperimetric function for Artin groups, the
defining graph of which contains no edges labelled by 3. This in particular
shows that even Artin groups have solvable word problem. We use small
cancellation theory of relative extended presentations.

</details>

### [136] [Byzantine-Resilient Distributed Computation via Task Replication and Local Computations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16014)
*Aayush Rajesh,Nikhil Karamchandani,Vinod M. Prabhakaran*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 研究了在存在拜占庭工作节点的分布式计算环境中，中央节点通过任务复制和最少本地计算来解决独立子任务的问题，提出了一个在无通信约束下使用最优本地计算数量的协议，并进一步改进了通信效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在分布式计算系统中，当存在拜占庭故障工作节点时，中央节点需要可靠地完成由多个独立子任务组成的计算任务，同时希望最小化昂贵的本地计算开销，这需要设计有效的任务分配和容错机制。

Method: 提出了一个基于任务复制的分布式计算协议，通过平衡的工作分配策略，将子任务分配给多个工作节点进行冗余计算，同时中央节点执行少量本地计算作为备份，并针对循环分配模式进行了专门的性能分析和协议改进。

Result: 对于一般的平衡工作分配，该协议能够在无通信约束条件下使用最优数量的本地计算成功解决所有子任务；对循环分配提供了封闭形式的性能结果；改进的协议在不增加本地计算量的前提下提高了通信效率。

Conclusion: 该研究成功设计了一个在拜占庭环境下的分布式计算协议，实现了本地计算数量的最优化，并在保持计算效率的同时改善了通信性能，为容错分布式计算系统提供了理论基础和实用解决方案。

Abstract: We study a distributed computation problem in the presence of Byzantine
workers where a central node wishes to solve a task that is divided into
independent sub-tasks, each of which needs to be solved correctly. The
distributed computation is achieved by allocating the sub-task computation
across workers with replication, as well as solving a small number of sub-tasks
locally, which we wish to minimize due to it being expensive. For a general
balanced job allocation, we propose a protocol that successfully solves for all
sub-tasks using an optimal number of local computations under no communication
constraints. Closed-form performance results are presented for cyclic
allocations. Furthermore, we propose a modification to this protocol to improve
communication efficiency without compromising on the amount of local
computation.

### [137] [Constructions and List Decoding of Sum-Rank Metric Codes Based on Orthogonal Spaces over Finite Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16377)
*Xuemei Liu,Jiarong Zhang,Gang Wang*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本研究基于有限域上的正交空间构造了sum-rank度量码，并计算了不同解码算法的列表大小，通过构造循环和非循环正交群，提出了两种构造方法，并利用子空间设计改进了解码成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Sum-rank度量码作为汉明码和秩度量码的推广，在多镜头线性网络编码、空时编码和分布式存储系统等领域有重要应用，需要研究基于有限域正交空间的构造方法和解码算法性能。

Method: 基于有限域上本原多项式的伴随矩阵构造了阶为q^n-1的循环正交群和阶为(q^n-1)^2的阿贝尔非循环正交群；通过选择不同的子空间生成矩阵构造最大秩距离(MRD)码；提出两种sum-rank度量码构造方法；使用[n,k,d]_{q^n/q}系统将sum-rank度量码与子空间设计关联。

Result: 成功构造了参数为(n×2n, q^{2n}, n)_q和(n×4n, q^{4n}, n)_q的MRD码；计算了列表解码算法下的列表大小；基于子空间设计的计算方法相比传统方法提高了解码成功率。

Conclusion: 通过正交空间理论成功构造了sum-rank度量码，提出的基于子空间设计的列表大小计算方法能够有效改善解码性能，为相关应用领域提供了理论基础和实用方法。

Abstract: Sum-rank metric codes, as a generalization of Hamming codes and rank metric
codes, have important applications in fields such as multi-shot linear network
coding, space-time coding and distributed storage systems. The purpose of this
study is to construct sum-rank metric codes based on orthogonal spaces over
finite fields, and calculate the list sizes outputted by different decoding
algorithms. The following achievements have been obtained.
  In this study, we construct a cyclic orthogonal group of order $q^n-1$ and an
Abelian non-cyclic orthogonal group of order $(q^n-1)^2$ based on the companion
matrices of primitive polynomials over finite fields. By selecting different
subspace generating matrices, maximum rank distance (MRD) codes with parameters
$(n \times {2n}, q^{2n}, n)_q$ and $(n \times {4n}, q^{4n}, n)_q$ are
constructed respectively. Two methods for constructing sum-rank metric codes
are proposed for the constructed MRD codes, and the list sizes outputted under
the list decoding algorithm are calculated. Subsequently, the
$[{\bf{n}},k,d]_{{q^n}/q}$-system is used to relate sum-rank metric codes to
subspace designs. The list size of sum-rank metric codes under the list
decoding algorithm is calculated based on subspace designs. This calculation
method improves the decoding success rate compared with traditional methods.
