### [138] [Typicality with Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16384)
*Thomas Sturma,Michèle Wigger*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文分析了发射机可以根据先前信道输出自适应调整输入的闭环反馈系统，证明了无论发射机采用何种策略，输出的条件类型都接近于离散无记忆信道的转移律，并将此结果应用于集成感知与通信系统，表明闭环系统的基本限制与开环系统相同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究发射机能够基于先前信道输出进行自适应输入调整的闭环反馈系统的基本性质，并探索这类自适应系统在集成感知与通信应用中的基本限制。

Method: 通过理论分析证明在闭环反馈系统中，给定输入条件下输出的条件类型始终接近离散无记忆信道的转移律P_{Y|X}，然后将此一般性结果应用于集成感知与通信模型的分析。

Result: 证明了无论发射机策略如何，条件类型都保持接近DMC转移律；在ISAC应用中，当可容许平均解码错误概率ε和可容许超额失真概率δ的和小于1时，闭环系统的基本限制与开环系统相同。

Conclusion: 闭环反馈系统中的条件类型稳定性为研究自适应系统的基本限制提供了理论基础，在集成感知与通信系统中，反馈信号虽然可用于状态估计，但不会改变系统的基本通信限制。

Abstract: The main objective of this paper is to analyze a closed-loop feedback system
where a transmitter probes a discrete memoryless channel (DMC) and can adapt
its inputs based on the previous channel outputs. We prove that, regardless of
the transmitter's strategy, the conditional type of the outputs given the
inputs remains close to the DMC transition law $P_{Y|X}$. This general result
enables the study of fundamental limits in certain adaptive systems.
  As an application, we establish a converse result for an integrated sensing
and communication (ISAC) model. In this setting, the transmitter also functions
as a radar receiver, aiming to simultaneously transmit a message over the
channel and estimate the channel state from the backscattered feedback signals.
We show that the fundamental limits of the closed loop system are the same as
of the open-loop system where the transmitter can use the feedback signal to
estimate the state but not to produce adaptive channel inputs. This result
holds as long as the sum of the admissible-average-decoding-error-probability,
denoted $\epsilon$, and the admissible-excess-distortion-probability, denoted
$\delta$, is below $1$, i.e., $\delta +\epsilon < 1$.

</details>


### [139] [Active RISs: Modeling and Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16499)
*Recep Akif Tasci,Panagiotis Gavriilidis,Ertugrul Basar,George C. Alexandropoulos*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究了主动可重构智能表面(Active RIS)技术，通过功率放大器和隧道二极管两种硬件设计克服传统RIS的双路径损耗问题，建立了数学模型并优化了系统性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统可重构智能表面受到双路径损耗效应的根本限制，严重衰减反射信号，需要开发能够放大入射信号的主动RIS架构来克服这一局限性。

Method: 研究了两种主动RIS硬件设计：1)基于单个功率放大器的双RIS结构；2)使用隧道二极管的单元级反射放大结构。建立了综合数学模型，推导了信噪比、误码率和能效的闭式表达式，提出了相位移和放大器增益的优化框架。

Result: 理论分析和数值仿真验证表明，主动RIS能够有效克服双路径损耗限制，相比被动RIS实现更好的能效权衡。同时发现更多的主动元件数量并不总是带来最优性能。

Conclusion: 主动RIS技术通过信号放大能力成功解决了传统RIS的双路径损耗问题，在功率约束下能够显著提升系统容量和能效，为下一代无线网络提供了变革性的解决方案。

Abstract: Reconfigurable Intelligent Surfaces (RIS)-empowered communication has emerged
as a transformative technology for next generation wireless networks, enabling
the programmable shaping of the propagation environment. However, conventional
RISs are fundamentally limited by the double path loss effect, which severely
attenuates the reflected signals. To overcome this, active RIS architectures,
capable of amplifying impinging signals, have been proposed. This chapter
investigates the modeling, performance analysis, and optimization of active
RISs, focusing on two hardware designs: a dual-RIS structure with a single
Power Amplifier (PA), and a reflection amplification structure at the unit cell
level using tunnel diodes. For the PA-based design, a comprehensive
mathematical model is developed, and closed-form expressions for the received
signal-to-noise ratio, bit error probability, and Energy Efficiency (EE) are
derived. An optimization framework for configuring the phase shifts and
amplifier gain is proposed to maximize system capacity under power constraints.
Regarding the second design, the integration of a tunnel diode into the unit
cell is carefully studied by analyzing its I-V characteristic, enabling the
derivation of the negative resistance range and the power consumption model.
Furthermore, the intrinsic phase-amplitude coupling of the reflection
coefficient is characterized through compact linear algebra formulations,
enabling practical optimization of active RISs. Extensive numerical simulations
validate the theoretical analyses, demonstrating that active RISs can
effectively overcome the double path loss limitation and achieve favorable EE
trade-offs compared to passive RISs. Finally, the trade-off between the
available power budget and the number of active elements is examined, revealing
that a higher number of active elements does not always lead to optimal
performance.

</details>


### [140] [A Robust 5G Terrestrial Positioning System with Sensor Fusion in GNSS-denied Scenarios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16600)
*Hamed Talebian,Nazrul Mohamed Nazeer,Darius Chmieliauskas,Jakub Nikonowicz,Mehdi Haghshenas,Łukasz Matuszewski,Mairo Leier,Aamir Mahmood*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于5G基础设施的地面定位系统，作为GNSS的可行替代方案，特别适用于GNSS信号被遮挡或不可用的场景。该系统结合载波相位测距和三边测量技术，在城市环境中可实现小于5米的定位精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统GNSS系统在信号被遮挡或不可用的环境中存在局限性，需要开发一种可靠的替代定位方案。现有地面网络主要针对通信服务优化，而非定位服务，因此需要重新设计网络规划以支持高精度定位作为主要服务。

Method: 系统采用多载波相位(CP)测距结合三边测量进行定位；使用多载波CP方法消除整数模糊度估计需求；开发深度学习模型识别并排除非视距(NLOS)链路；在视距受阻情况下，采用误差状态扩展卡尔曼滤波器融合IMU和相机等传感器数据；通过混合方法实现在不同信道条件下对移动用户的鲁棒跟踪。

Result: 在真实世界KITTI数据集上的仿真结果显示，该系统在城市环境中可实现小于5米的定位误差，其精度可与公共商用GNSS服务相媲美，证明了系统在GNSS拒止环境中的潜力。

Conclusion: 基于5G基础设施的地面定位系统为GNSS拒止环境提供了一种弹性且准确的解决方案。通过网络规划优化、多载波相位测距、深度学习NLOS识别和多传感器融合等技术，该系统能够在复杂城市环境中实现与商用GNSS相当的定位精度。

Abstract: This paper presents a terrestrial localization system based on 5G
infrastructure as a viable alternative to GNSS, particularly in scenarios where
GNSS signals are obstructed or unavailable. It discusses network planning aimed
at enabling positioning as a primary service, in contrast to the traditional
focus on communication services in terrestrial networks. Building on a network
infrastructure optimized for positioning, the paper proposes a system that
leverages carrier phase (CP) ranging in combination with trilateration to
localize the user within the network when at least three base stations (BSs)
provide line-of-sight (LOS) conditions. Achieving accurate CP-based positioning
requires addressing three key challenges: integer ambiguity resolution,
LOS/NLOS link identification, and localization under obstructed LOS conditions.
To this end, the system employs a multi-carrier CP approach, which eliminates
the need for explicit integer ambiguity estimation. Additionally, a deep
learning model is developed to identify NLOS links and exclude them from the
trilateration process. In cases where LOS is obstructed and CP ranging becomes
unreliable, the system incorporates an error-state extended Kalman filter to
fuse complementary data from other sensors, such as inertial measurement units
(IMUs) and cameras. This hybrid approach enables robust tracking of moving
users across diverse channel conditions. The performance of the proposed
terrestrial positioning system is evaluated using the real-world KITTI dataset,
featuring a moving vehicle in an urban environment. Simulation results show
that the system can achieve a positioning error of less than 5 meters in the
KITTI urban scenario--comparable to that of public commercial GNSS
services--highlighting its potential as a resilient and accurate solution for
GNSS-denied environments.

</details>


### [141] [Reconfigurable Intelligent Surface-Enabled Green and Secure Offloading for Mobile Edge Computing Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16666)
*Tong-Xing Zheng,Xinji Wang,Xin Chen,Di Mao,Jia Shi,Cunhua Pan,Chongwen Huang,Haiyang Ding,Zan Li*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文研究了在多天线窃听者威胁下，利用可重配置智能表面(RIS)辅助的多用户上行移动边缘计算网络中的安全任务卸载问题，提出了基于块坐标下降的优化算法来最小化总能耗，并证明了RIS可以节省高达60%的能耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在移动边缘计算网络中，用户需要在多天线窃听者存在的威胁环境下安全地卸载计算任务，同时要考虑能耗优化。现有方案缺乏对可重配置智能表面在安全能效优化中作用的深入研究，需要设计既能保证安全性又能实现能效优化的解决方案。

Method: 建立了一个非凸优化问题来最小化总能耗，采用块坐标下降框架迭代优化用户本地计算比特数和传输功率、RIS相位偏移以及接入点的多用户检测矩阵。针对完美信道状态信息情况，使用逐次凸近似、半定规划和半定松弛技术；对于不完美信道状态信息情况，采用S-procedure和惩罚凸凹方法实现鲁棒设计。

Result: 提出的算法收敛性良好且有效。RIS在实现安全节能的移动边缘计算网络中发挥重要作用，与无RIS情况相比，部署良好设计的RIS可以节省高达60%的能耗。研究还揭示了RIS元素数量和部署位置、用户数量、任务规模和持续时间、信道状态信息不完善程度等关键因素对保密能效的影响。

Conclusion: RIS在多用户上行移动边缘计算网络中能够显著提升安全性和能效性能。通过合理的优化设计，RIS辅助的系统可以在保证安全卸载要求的同时大幅降低能耗，为未来移动边缘计算网络的安全节能设计提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: This paper investigates a multi-user uplink mobile edge computing (MEC)
network, where the users offload partial tasks securely to an access point
under the non-orthogonal multiple access policy with the aid of a
reconfigurable intelligent surface (RIS) against a multi-antenna eavesdropper.
We formulate a non-convex optimization problem of minimizing the total energy
consumption subject to secure offloading requirement, and we build an efficient
block coordinate descent framework to iteratively optimize the number of local
computation bits and transmit power at the users, the RIS phase shifts, and the
multi-user detection matrix at the access point. Specifically, we successively
adopt successive convex approximation, semi-definite programming, and
semidefinite relaxation to solve the problem with perfect eavesdropper's
channel state information (CSI), and we then employ S-procedure and penalty
convex-concave to achieve robust design for the imperfect CSI case. We provide
extensive numerical results to validate the convergence and effectiveness of
the proposed algorithms. We demonstrate that RIS plays a significant role in
realizing a secure and energy-efficient MEC network, and deploying a
well-designed RIS can save energy consumption by up to 60\% compared to that
without RIS. We further reveal impacts of various key factors on the secrecy
energy efficiency, including RIS element number and deployment position, user
number, task scale and duration, and CSI imperfection.

</details>

Abstract: Successive cancellation list (SCL) decoding has been widely adopted for polar

to SCL decoding can implement Forney's generalized decoding rule. Hence, it
provides an efficient means to discard unreliable decisions. The performance

analyzed via Monte Carlo simulations.

### [143] [Multi-RIS-Empowered Communication Systems: Capacity Analysis and Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16767)
*Aris L. Moustakas,George C. Alexandropoulos*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文使用统计物理方法推导了多天线收发器在多个可重构智能表面(RIS)环境下互信息的均值和方差的渐近闭式表达式，并提出了无需暴力数值优化的RIS优化方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在快衰落条件下，信道估计具有挑战性，需要开发不依赖精确信道知识的RIS优化方法。现有方法通常需要复杂的数值优化，缺乏对RIS系统统计特性的深入理解。

Method: 采用统计物理方法推导多RIS环境下互信息的渐近闭式表达式；基于大系统极限理论建立互信息的高斯近似模型；分析RIS处入射和出射信号相关矩阵的渐近特性；利用这些特性进行统计RIS优化而非暴力数值搜索。

Result: 推导的高斯近似在中等规模天线阵列和超表面情况下仍保持较高精度；当RIS附近信道相关时（如载波频率增加导致的小角度扩散），统计RIS优化带来的增益显著高于近似不相关情况；即使RIS的期望反射显著偏离几何光学预测，超表面仍可优化以提供鲁棒通信链路。

Conclusion: 统计物理方法能够有效分析多RIS系统的互信息特性，基于相关矩阵渐近特性的RIS优化方法避免了复杂的数值优化，在相关信道环境下能获得显著的性能增益，且不需要RIS的最优放置就能实现鲁棒通信。

Abstract: In this chapter, using statistical physics methods, asymptotic closed-form
expressions for the mean and variance of the mutual information for a
multi-antenna transmitter-receiver pair in the presence of multiple
Reconfigurable Intelligent Surfaces (RISs) are presented. While nominally valid
in the large-system limit, it is shown that the derived Gaussian approximation
for the mutual information can be quite accurate, even for modest-sized antenna
arrays and metasurfaces. The above results are particularly useful when
fast-fading conditions are present, which renders channel estimation
challenging. The derived analysis indicates that, when the channel close to an
RIS is correlated, for instance due to small angle spread which is reasonable
for wireless systems with increasing carrier frequencies, the communication
link benefits significantly from statistical RIS optimization, resulting in
gains that are surprisingly higher than the nearly uncorrelated case. More
importantly, the presented novel asymptotic properties of the correlation
matrices of the impinging and outgoing signals at the RISs can be deployed to
optimize the metasurfaces without brute-force numerical optimization. The
numerical investigation demonstrates that, when the desired reflection from any
of the RISs departs significantly from geometrical optics, the metasurfaces can
be optimized to provide robust communication links, without significant need
for their optimal placement.

</details>

### [144] [Homology of Epsilon-Strongly Graded Algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16778)
*Emmanuel Jerez*

TL;DR: 本文构造了收敛到分次代数Hochschild上同调的谱序列，并证明了该谱序列可以用群的部分上同调来表示，且在共轭类分解下可与相应中心化子的群同调等同。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构造谱序列技术，利用部分群上同调理论，结合全局化函子和共轭类分解方法来分析强G-分次代数的Hochschild上同调。

Result: 成功构造了收敛到Hochschild上同调的谱序列，证明了同调谱序列按群G的共轭类分解，并通过全局化函子将E²-页与适当中心化子的普通群同调等同起来。

Conclusion: 建立了强分次代数的Hochschild上同调与群论结构之间的深层联系，为计算此类代数的上同调提供了有效的群论工具和方法。

Abstract: Let $G$ be a group and $S$ a unital epsilon-strongly $G$-graded algebra. We
construct spectral sequences converging to the Hochschild (co)homology of $S$.
Each spectral sequence is expressed in terms of the partial group (co)homology
of $G$ with coefficients in the Hochschild (co)homology of the degree-one
component of $S$. Moreover, we show that the homology spectral sequence
decomposes according to the conjugacy classes of $G$, and, by means of the
globalization functor, its $E^2$-page can be identified with the ordinary group
homology of suitable centralizers.

### [145] [Singularities of Dirac-Coulomb propagators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16085)
*Dean Baskin,Michał Wrochna,Jared Wunsch*

TL;DR: 本文研究库仑势中狄拉克场的传播子和N点函数的奇异性，证明了进出狄拉克-库仑真空态是Hadamard态，并利用衍射奇异性传播定理分析了时间依赖势的情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究库仑势中狄拉克场的量子场论性质，特别是传播子和N点函数的奇异性行为，以及不同Hadamard态之间的电荷密度关系。这对于理解带电粒子在库仑场中的量子行为具有重要意义。

Method: 基于作者之前建立的狄拉克-库仑系统的衍射奇异性传播定理，将其推广到时间依赖势的情况。通过数学分析方法研究传播子的奇异性结构，并分析Hadamard态的性质。

Result: 证明了当r≠0时，进出狄拉克-库仑真空态是Hadamard态。同时证明了任意两个Hadamard态的相对电荷密度在r=0附近作为局部可积函数是良定义的。这些结果适用于含有时间依赖光滑部分的库仑势。

Conclusion: 通过衍射奇异性传播定理的推广，成功建立了时间依赖库仑势中狄拉克场的严格数学框架。证明了Hadamard态的存在性和相对电荷密度的良定义性，为库仑势中的量子场论提供了坚实的数学基础。

Abstract: In this paper we study singularities of propagators and $N$-point functions
for Dirac fields in a Coulomb potential, possibly with a $t$-dependent smooth
part for $|t|<T<\infty$. We show that the in and out Dirac-Coulomb vacua are
Hadamard states for $r\neq 0$. Furthermore, we prove that the relative charge
density of any two Hadamard states is well-defined as a locally integrable
function including near $r=0$. The results are based on a diffractive
propagation of singularities theorem for the Dirac-Coulomb system previously
obtained by the first and third authors, generalized here to the case of
$t$-dependent potentials.

Result: 证明了当N趋向无穷大时，具有Slater初始数据的二维费米子系统在时间演化过程中保持其Slater结构。系统的波函数可以用Slater行列式近似，其轨道根据N个耦合的Chern-Simons-Schrödinger型有效方程演化。

Abstract: We show that a 2-dimensional system of N fermions interacting through a

preserves its Slater structure over time when N gets large. In other words, the

orbitals evolves according to a coupled system of N Chern-Simons- Schr\"odinger
type effective equations. The result holds in a dilute regime where the density
is of order one on a large volume proportional to the number of particles. The
pairwise magnetic feature of the system implies to deal with the
diagonalization of three-body potentials which is the main mathematical
innovation of the paper.

</details>

small values of the inverse P\'eclet number, the concentration varies from the
clean state of the adsorbent matrix to a full saturation. We present numerical
simulations to illustrate the analytical results for different P\'eclet number
values and conduct a sensitivity analysis that demonstrates the system's
robustness.

### [149] [Rigidity and positivity of Hawking quasi-local energy on area-constrained critical surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16588)
*Alejandro Peñuela Diaz*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了霍金能量在其自然约束临界面（霍金面）上满足非负性和刚性条件，为准局域能量在广义相对论中的物理合理性提供了重要理论支撑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义相对论中的准局域能量必须满足非负性和刚性条件（能量为零时区域必须是平坦的）才能被认为是物理上合理的。霍金能量作为重要的准局域能量概念，其是否满足这些基本物理原理一直存在争议和模糊性，需要严格的数学证明来澄清这些问题。

Method: 研究采用严格的数学分析方法，在主导能量条件下证明霍金能量在霍金面上的性质。对于时间对称情况，将霍金面与面积约束威尔莫尔面联系起来，扩展分析包含电荷、非零宇宙学常数和高维情况。对于完全动力学（非时间对称）情况，建立了霍金能量的非负性和刚性定理。

Result: 成功证明了霍金能量在霍金面上满足非负性和刚性条件。在时间对称情况下，这些性质被扩展到包含电荷、宇宙学常数和高维空间的情况。在完全动力学情况下，首次建立了霍金能量的非负性和刚性定理，这是该领域的重要突破。

Conclusion: 研究结果确认了霍金能量与基本物理原理的一致性，解决了长期存在的模糊性和批评。这为霍金能量作为广义相对论中有效的准局域能量概念提供了坚实的理论基础，推进了引力理论中能量概念的理解。

Abstract: A key test for any quasi-local energy in general relativity is that it be
nonnegative and satisfy a rigidity property; if it vanishes, the region
enclosed is flat. We show that the Hawking energy, when evaluated on its
natural area-constrained critical surfaces, henceforth called "Hawking
surfaces", satisfies both properties under the dominant energy condition. In
the time-symmetric case, where Hawking surfaces coincide with area-constrained
Willmore surfaces, we extend positivity and rigidity to include electric
charge, a nonzero cosmological constant, and higher dimensions. In the fully
dynamical (non-time-symmetric) case, we establish the first nonnegativity and
rigidity theorems for the Hawking energy in this general setting. These results
confirm the Hawking energy consistency with basic physical principles and
address several longstanding ambiguities and criticisms.

</details>

Conclusion: 建立了半单李群子群保持旗流形适当域的理论框架，通过因果凸性概念深化了对Hermitian李群Shilov边界几何结构的理解，为研究李群动力学提供了新的几何视角

Abstract: Given a semisimple Lie group $G$ and a self-opposite flag manifold
$\mathcal{F}$ of $G$, we establish a necessary condition for an infinite
subgroup $H$ of $G$ to preserve a proper domain in $\mathcal{F}$. In the case
where $G$ is a Hermitian Lie group of tube type, we introduce and study a
notion of causal convexity in the Shilov boundary $\mathbf{Sb}(G)$ of the
symmetric space of $G$, inspired by the one already existing in conformal
Lorentzian geometry. We show that subgroups $H$ of $G$ that are transverse with
respect to a parabolic subgroup of $G$ defining $\mathbf{Sb}(G)$ and that
preserve a proper domain in $\mathbf{Sb}(G)$ satisfy a geometric property with
respect to this causal convexity, close to the strong projective convex
cocompactness defined by Danciger--Gu\'eritaud--Kassel. This result highlights
the spatial nature of the dynamics of $H$. We construct Zariski-dense examples
of such transverse subgroups.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

non-symmetric analog of a Schur measure). LPP along a main diagonal, from
$(1,1)$ to $(n,n)$, is distributed as a marginal of a Pfaffian Schur process.

is governed by the GOE Tracy-Widom distribution, in the second case - by the
GSE Tracy-Widom distribution. In the latter case we were also able to study the

GSE Tracy-Widom distribution.

### [158] [Tilting theoretic approach to quasi-hereditary structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16575)
*Takahide Adachi,Aaron Chan,Yuta Kimura,Mayu Tsukamoto*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文研究了拟遗传代数中的特征倾斜模块，通过引入IS-倾斜模块的概念，完全刻画了哪些倾斜模块可以实现为特征倾斜模块，并应用于二次线性中山代数的分类和计数问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在拟遗传代数理论中，一个基本问题是确定哪些倾斜模块可以作为特征倾斜模块实现。虽然Ringel的经典结果表明拟遗传结构会产生特征倾斜模块，但反向问题——即给定倾斜模块何时为特征倾斜模块——仍未解决。

Method: 作者引入了IS-倾斜模块的概念，这是一个由倾斜模块T和其直和项上的偏序关系组成的对(T,⊴)，满足沿着偏序关系进行迭代幂等截断总是能揭示简单的直和项。通过这个新概念来刻画特征倾斜模块。

Result: 主要结果表明：倾斜模块T是特征倾斜模块当且仅当存在某个偏序关系⊴使得(T,⊴)是IS-倾斜的；此时有T=T_⊴。作为应用，证明了对于代数A，所有倾斜模块都是特征倾斜模块当且仅当A是二次线性中山代数。对于这类代数，给出了倾斜模块集合的分解和拟遗传结构的递归计数公式。

Conclusion: 本文通过IS-倾斜模块的概念完全解决了特征倾斜模块的刻画问题，建立了拟遗传结构与倾斜理论之间的桥梁。特别地，完全分类了所有倾斜模块都是特征倾斜模块的代数，并为二次线性中山代数的拟遗传结构提供了具体的描述和计数方法。

Abstract: A quasi-hereditary algebra is an algebra equipped with a certain partial
order $\unlhd$ on its simple modules. Such a partial order -- called a
quasi-hereditary structure -- gives rise to a characteristic tilting module
$T_{\unlhd}$ by a classical result due to Ringel. A fundamental question is to
determine which tilting modules can be realised as characteristic tilting
modules. We answer this question by using the notion of IS-tilting module,
which is a pair $(T,\unlhd)$ of a tilting module $T$ and a partial order
$\unlhd$ on its direct summands such that iterative idempotent truncation along
$\unlhd$ always reveals a simple direct summand. Specifically, we show that a
tilting module $T$ is characteristic if, and only if, there is some $\unlhd$ so
that $(T,\unlhd)$ is IS-tilting; in which case, we have $T=T_{\unlhd}$. This
result enables us to study quasi-hereditary structures using tilting theory.
  As an application of the above result, we show that, for an algebra $A$, all
tilting modules are characteristic if, and only if, $A$ is a quadratic linear
Nakayama algebra. Furthermore, for such an $A$, we provide a decomposition of
the set of its tilting modules that can be used to derive a recursive formula
for enumerating its quasi-hereditary structures. Finally, we describe the
quasi-hereditary structures of $A$ via `nodal gluing' and binary tree
sequences.

### [160] [Structured linear factor models for tail dependence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16340)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的稳定尾依赖函数参数模型中，线性和最大线性因子模型是一个重要子类，但在"纯变量假设"下估计因子数量K和因子载荷矩阵A面临挑战，特别是参数空间不符合常规估计框架，且需要处理维度可能大于样本量的高维情况。

Method: 提出两种算法来估计未知的因子数量K∈{1,...,d}和因子载荷矩阵A∈[0,∞)^(d×K)，这些算法专门设计用于处理非常规参数空间，并在"纯变量假设"的附加条件下工作。

Abstract: A common object to describe the extremal dependence of a $d$-variate random
vector $X$ is the stable tail dependence function $L$. Various parametric
models have emerged, with a popular subclass consisting of those stable tail
dependence functions that arise for linear and max-linear factor models with
heavy tailed factors. The stable tail dependence function is then parameterized
by a $d \times K$ matrix $A$, where $K$ is the number of factors and where $A$
can be interpreted as a factor loading matrix. We study estimation of $L$ under
an additional assumption on $A$ called the `pure variable assumption'. Both $K
\in \{1, \dots, d\}$ and $A \in [0, \infty)^{d \times K}$ are treated as
unknown, which constitutes an unconventional parameter space that does not fit
into common estimation frameworks. We suggest two algorithms that allow to
estimate $K$ and $A$, and provide finite sample guarantees for both algorithms.
Remarkably, the guarantees allow for the case where the dimension $d$ is larger
than the sample size $n$. The results are illustrated with numerical
experiments.

### [161] [Bayesian causal discovery: Posterior concentration and optimal detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16529)
*Valentinian Lungu,Joni Shaska,Ioannis Kontoyiannis,Urbashi Mitra*

Main category: math.ST

TL;DR: 本文研究线性结构方程模型中贝叶斯因果发现问题，发现当真实DAG为最大图时后验概率以指数速度收敛到1，否则收敛速度不超过1/√n，揭示了避免过拟合比识别所有结构更困难的现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线性结构方程模型框架下研究贝叶斯因果发现问题，特别关注后验分布在模型空间上的收敛性质，以及真实有向无环图(DAG)的性质如何影响这种收敛速度。

Method: 采用贝叶斯方法，在有向无环图空间上设置均匀先验，在给定图结构下对线性系数设置独立高斯先验，通过理论分析研究后验概率的收敛性质，并建立与边检测中最优假设检验的新联系。

Result: 发现了收敛速度的尖锐二分现象：如果真实DAG是最大的（添加任何新边都会违反无环性），则后验概率以指数速度收敛到1；否则收敛速度不超过1/√n。通过仿真实验验证了理论发现。

Conclusion: 揭示了贝叶斯因果发现中的一个重要现象：避免过拟合比识别模型中存在的所有结构要困难得多。这种尖锐的二分性质为理解因果发现的理论基础提供了新的见解。

Abstract: We consider the problem of Bayesian causal discovery for the standard model
of linear structural equations with equivariant Gaussian noise. A uniform prior
is placed on the space of directed acyclic graphs (DAGs) over a fixed set of
variables and, given the graph, independent Gaussian priors are placed on the
associated linear coefficients of pairwise interactions. We show that the rate
at which the posterior on model space concentrates on the true underlying DAG
depends critically on its nature: If it is maximal, in the sense that adding
any one new edge would violate acyclicity, then its posterior probability
converges to 1 exponentially fast (almost surely) in the sample size $n$.
Otherwise, it converges at a rate no faster than $1/\sqrt{n}$. This sharp
dichotomy is an instance of the important general phenomenon that avoiding
overfitting is significantly harder than identifying all of the structure that
is present in the model. We also draw a new connection between the posterior
distribution on model space and recent results on optimal hypothesis testing in
the related problem of edge detection. Our theoretical findings are illustrated
empirically through simulation experiments.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We study the Gaussian sequence model, i.e. $X \sim N(\mathbf{\theta},
I_\infty)$, where $\mathbf{\theta} \in \Gamma \subset \ell_2$ is assumed to be
convex and compact. We show that goodness-of-fit testing sample complexity is
lower bounded by the square-root of the estimation complexity, whenever
$\Gamma$ is orthosymmetric. We show that the lower bound is tight when $\Gamma$
is also quadratically convex, thus significantly extending validity of the
testing-estimation relationship from [GP24]. Using similar methods, we also
completely characterize likelihood-free hypothesis testing (LFHT) complexity
for $\ell_p$-bodies, discovering new types of tradeoff between the numbers of
simulation and observation samples.

### [163] [Can we have it all? Non-asymptotically valid and asymptotically exact confidence intervals for expectations and linear regressions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16776)
*Alexis Derumigny,Lucas Girard,Yannick Guyonvarch*

Main category: math.ST

TL;DR: 本文研究了在半参数统计模型上既非渐近有效又渐近精确一致(NAVAE)的置信集，提出了构造此类置信集的充分条件，并在标量期望和OLS系数线性组合两个标准设置下构造了闭式NAVAE置信区间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的置信集要么在有限样本下有效但渐近保守，要么渐近精确但有限样本性质不明确。本文旨在弥合大样本推断和有限样本推断之间的差距，寻找同时满足非渐近有效性和渐近精确性的置信集。

Method: 首先推导出构造NAVAE置信集的一般充分条件：只要存在一致渐近精确的置信集，就可以构造NAVAE置信集。然后基于这一联系，在仅有矩条件的约束下，为两个标准设置构造闭式NAVAE置信区间：(1)标量期望情况下仅需要有界峰度；(2)OLS系数线性组合情况下允许异方差和弱外生性。通过扩大基于中心极限定理的渐近精确置信区间来确保非渐近保证。

Result: 成功构造了在标量期望和OLS系数线性组合设置下的闭式NAVAE置信区间。这些置信区间在有限样本下保持有效性，同时在极限情况下与经典的渐近置信区间一致。通过仿真研究验证了方法的潜力和局限性。

Conclusion: 本文成功地在特定条件下构造了同时满足非渐近有效性和渐近精确性的置信区间，为弥合大样本和有限样本推断提供了新的理论工具。所提出的修正在渐近情况下消失，确保了与经典方法的一致性，同时在有限样本下提供了更可靠的推断保证。

Abstract: We contribute to bridging the gap between large- and finite-sample inference
by studying confidence sets (CSs) that are both non-asymptotically valid and
asymptotically exact uniformly (NAVAE) over semi-parametric statistical models.
NAVAE CSs are not easily obtained; for instance, we show they do not exist over
the set of Bernoulli distributions. We first derive a generic sufficient
condition: NAVAE CSs are available as soon as uniform asymptotically exact CSs
are. Second, building on that connection, we construct closed-form NAVAE
confidence intervals (CIs) in two standard settings -- scalar expectations and
linear combinations of OLS coefficients -- under moment conditions only. For
expectations, our sole requirement is a bounded kurtosis. In the OLS case, our
moment constraints accommodate heteroskedasticity and weak exogeneity of the
regressors. Under those conditions, we enlarge the Central Limit Theorem-based
CIs, which are asymptotically exact, to ensure non-asymptotic guarantees. Those
modifications vanish asymptotically so that our CIs coincide with the classical
ones in the limit. We illustrate the potential and limitations of our approach
through a simulation study.

</details>

### [164] [Exact Lagrangian fillability of 3-braid closures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16747)
*James Hughes,Jiajie Ma*

Main category: math.SG

TL;DR: 该研究确定了标准接触R³中Legendrian拟正3-辫闭包何时具有可定向或不可定向的精确拉格朗日填充，为Hayden和Sabloff的可定向填充性猜想提供了证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Legendrian拟正3-辫闭包的精确拉格朗日填充性质，特别是验证Hayden和Sabloff提出的可定向填充性猜想，这对理解接触几何和辛几何中的填充问题具有重要意义。

Method: 通过分析3-辫闭包的拟正性和HOMFLY多项式对最大Thurston-Bennequin数的界限，构造具有最大Thurston-Bennequin数的拟正3-辫闭包的显式Legendrian代表，并研究其填充性质。

Result: 证明了3-辫闭包是可定向精确拉格朗日可填充的当且仅当它是拟正的且HOMFLY界限对其最大Thurston-Bennequin数是紧的。同时构造了具有最大Thurston-Bennequin数的拟正3-辫闭包的显式Legendrian代表。

Conclusion: 该研究为Hayden和Sabloff的可定向填充性猜想提供了强有力的证据，建立了3-辫闭包的可定向精确拉格朗日填充性与其拟正性和HOMFLY界限紧性之间的等价关系，并提供了相关的显式构造方法。

Abstract: We determine when a Legendrian quasipositive 3-braid closure in standard
contact $\mathbb{R}^3$ admits an orientable or non-orientable exact Lagrangian
filling. Our main result provides evidence for the orientable fillability
conjecture of Hayden and Sabloff, showing that a 3-braid closure is orientably
exact Lagrangian fillable if and only if it is quasipositive and the HOMFLY
bound on its maximum Thurston-Bennequin number is sharp. Of possible
independent interest, we construct explicit Legendrian representatives of
quasipositive 3-braid closures with maximum Thurston-Bennequin number.

</details>

### [165] [A note on the boundary dynamics of holomorphic iterated function systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16358)
*Argyrios Christodoulou*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文研究了单位圆盘全纯自映射的迭代函数系统的边界动力学，提供了一个充分条件来保证左迭代函数系统在单位圆盘内部的动力学行为可以扩展到边界，将经典的Denjoy-Wolff定理的推广扩展到迭代函数系统设置中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将经典的Denjoy-Wolff定理（由Bourdon, Matache和Shapiro推广）从单个全纯自映射扩展到迭代函数系统的设置中，特别是研究左迭代函数系统从单位圆盘内部到边界的动力学行为扩展问题。

Method: 修改复合算子Hardy范数的估计方法，并结合一种新的技术——通过椭圆Möbius变换扰动左迭代函数系统，来分析边界动力学行为。

Result: 获得了一个充分条件，该条件能够保证左迭代函数系统在单位圆盘内部的动力学行为可以成功扩展到边界上，从而实现了经典结果在迭代函数系统框架下的推广。

Conclusion: 成功将经典的Denjoy-Wolff定理推广到迭代函数系统的边界动力学研究中，通过新的技术方法建立了内部动力学行为向边界扩展的充分条件，为复动力系统理论提供了重要的理论贡献。

Abstract: We consider the boundary dynamics of iterated function systems of holomorphic
self-maps of the unit disc. Our main result provides a sufficient condition
which guarantees that the dynamical behaviour of a left iterated function
system in the interior of the unit disc can be extended to the boundary. This
generalises an extension of the classical Denjoy--Wolff Theorem, due to
Bourdon, Matache and Shapiro, to the setting of iterated function systems. To
do so we modify estimates for the Hardy norm of composition operators and
combine them with a new technique of perturbing a left iterated function system
by elliptic M\"obius transformations.

### [166] [Asymptotic consensus with transmission and reaction delay: an overview](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16072)
*Jan Haskovec*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文系统性地分析了带延迟的Hegselmann-Krause型模型的渐近一致性问题，区分了传输延迟和反应延迟两种类型，并针对不同场景提出了四个定理和相应的证明方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的Hegselmann-Krause一致性模型缺乏对延迟因素的系统性分析，而在实际系统中延迟是普遍存在的重要因素，因此需要建立一个完整的理论框架来理解延迟对一致性收敛的影响。

Method: 通过区分传输延迟和反应延迟两种类型，分别考虑经典和归一化通信权重，使用双智能体玩具模型建立直观理解，然后针对四种不同场景分别采用直接估计法、凸性论证、Lyapunov泛函和广义Gronwall-Halanay不等式等分析工具进行理论证明。

Result: 建立了四个渐近一致性定理：(1)传输延迟+经典权重、(2)传输延迟+归一化权重、(3)反应延迟+对称权重、(4)反应延迟+非对称权重。发现传输延迟下任意长度延迟都能达到一致性，而反应延迟需要延迟足够小才能保证一致性。

Conclusion: 传输延迟和反应延迟对系统一致性的影响机制不同：传输延迟对一致性收敛具有鲁棒性，而反应延迟则对延迟长度敏感。不同场景需要采用不同的数学分析工具，为带延迟的多智能体一致性问题提供了完整的理论基础。

Abstract: The aim of this paper is to provide a systematic overview of results on
asymptotic consensus for the Hegselmann-Krause-type model with delay and
discuss the corresponding analytical tools. We explain that two types (sources)
of delay - transmission and reaction - are justifiable from the modeling point
of view. We consider both classical and normalized communication weights.
Studying a toy model with two agents only, we develop an intuitive insight into
what type of dynamics we can expect from the systems. In particular, we stress
that with transmission-type delay, asymptotic consensus can be reached with any
length of the delay (i.e., without smallness assumptions). In contrast, the
systems with reaction-type delay can only reach asymptotic consensus if the
delay is sufficiently small.
  We formulate four theorems that establish asymptotic consensus in the
following scenarios: (1) transmission-type delay with classical communication
weights, (2) transmission-type delay with normalized communication weights, (3)
reaction-type delay with symmetric communication weights, (4) reaction-type
delay with non-symmetric communication weights.
  We explain how the methods of proof depend on the particular scenario: direct
estimates for (1), convexity arguments for (2), Lyapunov functional for (3) and
generalized Gronwall-Halanay inequality for (4).

</details>

*Peter H Baxendale*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立随机微分方程在流形上有限时间李雅普诺夫指数的大偏差理论，特别是将紧致流形的结果推广到非紧致情况，并研究相关的中心极限定理和中偏差估计。

Method: 利用Gartner-Ellis定理将大偏差速率函数与p阶矩李雅普诺夫指数联系起来；对于紧致流形，通过单位球束上微分算子的特征值问题来刻画矩指数；对于非紧致情况，制定增长条件结合椭圆性和正性假设，确保特征值刻画在适当函数空间中仍然有效。

Result: 获得了有限时间李雅普诺夫指数的中心极限定理和中偏差估计，这些结果都涉及矩指数函数在0点的二阶导数；建立了非紧致流形情况下特征值问题的有效性条件。

Conclusion: 成功将紧致流形上的李雅普诺夫指数大偏差理论推广到非紧致情况，通过适当的增长条件和函数空间限制，保证了特征值刻画方法的有效性，并得到了相应的概率极限定理。

Abstract: The rate function for large deviations of the finite time Lyapunov exponent
for the derived process in TM corresponding to a stochastic differential
equation in M is related, via the Gartner-Ellis theorem, to the p-th moment
Lyapunov exponent. When M is compact there is a characterization of the p-th
moment Lyapunov exponent in terms of an eigenvalue problem for an associated
differential operator acting on functions on the unit sphere bundle SM. For the
non-compact case, we formulate growth conditions which, together with standard
assumptions of hypoellipticity and positivity, ensure that the eigenvalue
characterization remains valid so long as the corresponding eigenfunction is
restricted to be in a suitable function space. There is a central limit theorem
for finite time Lyapunov exponent, and there are moderate deviation estimates
for the finite time Lyapunov exponent, both involving the second derivative of
the moment exponent function at 0.

</details>


### [168] [From heteroclinic loops to homoclinic snaking in reversible systems: rigorous forcing through computer-assisted proofs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16798)
*Jan Bouwe van den Berg,Gabriel William Duchesne,Jean-Philippe Lessard*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文使用计算机辅助证明方法，在Swift-Hohenberg和Gray-Scott问题中证明了同宿蛇形现象的存在，为理解非线性动力系统的全局动力学提供了强有力的工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 同宿蛇形现象在许多模式形成系统中广泛存在，但在非扰动条件下证明其存在性一直很困难。虽然已有基于模式化前沿解的强迫理论，但这些异宿解本身由于问题的非线性特性而难以分析。

Method: 采用计算机辅助证明方法，在时间可逆系统中寻找平衡点和周期轨道之间异宿连接的参数化环路。

Result: 成功在Swift-Hohenberg和Gray-Scott问题中证明了同宿蛇形现象的存在。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，计算机辅助证明连续族连接轨道在非线性动力系统中是理解全局动力学及其参数依赖性的强有力工具。

Abstract: Homoclinic snaking is a widespread phenomenon observed in many
pattern-forming systems. Demonstrating its occurrence in non-perturbative
regimes has proven difficult, although a forcing theory has been developed
based on the identification of patterned front solutions. These heteroclinic
solutions are themselves challenging to analyze due to the nonlinear nature of
the problem. In this paper, we use computer-assisted proofs to find
parameterized loops of heteroclinic connections between equilibria and periodic
orbits in time reversible systems. This leads to a proof of homoclinic snaking
in both the Swift-Hohenberg and Gray-Scott problems. Our results demonstrate
that computer-assisted proofs of continuous families of connecting orbits in
nonlinear dynamical systems are a powerful tool for understanding global
dynamics and their dependence on parameters.

</details>

### [169] [Mass-gap description of heavy impurities in Fermi gases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.15957)
*Xin Chen,Eugen Dizer,Emilio Ramos Rodríguez,Richard Schmidt*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个统一理论，连接了移动杂质的费米极化子准粒子图像与静态杂质的安德森正交灾变，通过算符重排序获得了带有反冲诱导能隙（质量能隙）的修正费米子色散关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论中，移动杂质的费米极化子准粒子图像与静态杂质的安德森正交灾变之间缺乏统一的理论连接，需要建立一个能够解释这两种现象共同微观起源的理论框架。

Method: 通过对底层多体哈密顿量进行算符重排序，获得修正的费米子色散关系，该关系具有反冲诱导的能隙（称为"质量能隙"）。基于此构建平均场哈密顿量，分析有限杂质质量情况下的能隙内态。

Result: 发现所得的平均场哈密顿量在有限杂质质量时展现出能隙内态，该态在费米极化子和分子形成中起关键作用。确定了质量能隙是费米极化子准粒子权重的微观起源，并推导出权重与杂质-费米子质量比的幂律标度关系。

Conclusion: 质量能隙及其相关的能隙内态提供了费米极化子准粒子权重的微观解释，并且该能隙内态导致了极化子-分子转变的出现，这与安德森正交灾变的极限情况（转变不存在）形成对比，从而建立了两种物理现象之间的统一理论连接。

Abstract: We present a unified theory that connects the quasiparticle picture of Fermi
polarons for mobile impurities to the Anderson orthogonality catastrophe for
static impurities. By operator reordering of the underlying many-body
Hamiltonian, we obtain a modified fermionic dispersion relation that features a
recoil-induced energy gap, which we call the `mass gap'. We show that the
resulting mean-field Hamiltonian exhibits an in-gap state for finite impurity
mass, which takes a key role in Fermi polaron and molecule formation. We
identify the mass gap as the microscopic origin of the quasiparticle weight of
Fermi polarons and derive a power-law scaling of the weight with the
impurity-to-fermion mass ratio. The associated in-gap state is shown to give
rise to the emergence of the polaron-to-molecule transition away from the
limiting case of the Anderson orthogonality catastrophe in which the transition
is absent.

</details>

Abstract: We show that the perfect matching function on $n$-vertex graphs requires
monotone circuits of size $\smash{2^{n^{\Omega(1)}}}$. This improves on the

standard approximation method together with a new sunflower lemma for
matchings.

### [173] [Latent Space Alignment for AI-Native MIMO Semantic Communications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16680)
*Mario Edoardo Pandolfo,Simone Fiorellino,Emilio Calvanese Strinati,Paolo Di Lorenzo*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用MIMO通信解决语义通信中潜在空间不匹配问题的新方法，通过学习MIMO预编码器/解码器对来同时执行潜在空间压缩和语义信道均衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在语义通信中，当设备使用不同的语言、逻辑或内部表示时，会出现语义不匹配问题，这可能阻碍相互理解。现有方法难以同时处理语义不匹配和物理信道损害问题。

Method: 提出两种解决方案：(1)线性模型，通过交替方向乘数法(ADMM)求解双凸优化问题；(2)基于神经网络的模型，在传输功率预算和复杂度约束下学习语义MIMO预编码器/解码器。该方法学习MIMO预编码器/解码器对，联合执行潜在空间压缩和语义信道均衡。

Result: 数值结果表明所提方法在面向目标的语义通信场景中的有效性，展示了准确性、通信负担和解决方案复杂性之间的主要权衡关系。

Conclusion: 该方法能够有效缓解语义不匹配和物理信道损害问题，在语义通信系统中实现了准确性、通信效率和计算复杂度之间的良好平衡。

Abstract: Semantic communications focus on prioritizing the understanding of the
meaning behind transmitted data and ensuring the successful completion of tasks
that motivate the exchange of information. However, when devices rely on
different languages, logic, or internal representations, semantic mismatches
may occur, potentially hindering mutual understanding. This paper introduces a
novel approach to addressing latent space misalignment in semantic
communications, exploiting multiple-input multiple-output (MIMO)
communications. Specifically, our method learns a MIMO precoder/decoder pair
that jointly performs latent space compression and semantic channel
equalization, mitigating both semantic mismatches and physical channel
impairments. We explore two solutions: (i) a linear model, optimized by solving
a biconvex optimization problem via the alternating direction method of
multipliers (ADMM); (ii) a neural network-based model, which learns semantic
MIMO precoder/decoder under transmission power budget and complexity
constraints. Numerical results demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed
approach in a goal-oriented semantic communication scenario, illustrating the
main trade-offs between accuracy, communication burden, and complexity of the
solutions.

</details>


### [174] [Enhancing Stability of Physics-Informed Neural Network Training Through Saddle-Point Reformulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16008)
*Dmitry Bylinkin,Mikhail Aleksandrov,Savelii Chezhegov,Aleksandr Beznosikov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文将物理信息神经网络(PINN)的训练重新表述为非凸-强凹鞍点问题，以解决其性能不稳定的问题，实验结果表明该方法优于现有最先进技术。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理信息神经网络(PINNs)虽然在多个应用中表现出色，但由于损失函数的复杂景观导致其性能仍然不稳定，需要寻找更稳定有效的训练方法。

Method: 将PINN训练重新表述为非凸-强凹鞍点问题，并为这种方法建立了理论基础。

Result: 通过在各种任务和架构上进行广泛的实验研究，证明了所提出方法的有效性，结果显示该方法优于当前最先进的技术。

Conclusion: 通过将PINN训练重新表述为鞍点问题，成功解决了传统PINN训练中的性能不稳定问题，为物理信息神经网络的训练提供了一种更加稳定和有效的新方法。

Abstract: Physics-informed neural networks (PINNs) have gained prominence in recent
years and are now effectively used in a number of applications. However, their
performance remains unstable due to the complex landscape of the loss function.
To address this issue, we reformulate PINN training as a nonconvex-strongly
concave saddle-point problem. After establishing the theoretical foundation for
this approach, we conduct an extensive experimental study, evaluating its
effectiveness across various tasks and architectures. Our results demonstrate
that the proposed method outperforms the current state-of-the-art techniques.

### [175] [Canonical Representations of Markovian Structural Causal Models: A Framework for Counterfactual Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16370)
*Lucas de Lara*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的反事实模型方法，作为结构因果模型的替代方案，用于表示与给定因果图模型兼容的反事实推理，并通过规范化程序实现各种反事实概念的描述和实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反事实推理是因果关系中最精细的层次，虽然许多反事实陈述无法被证伪（即使通过随机实验），但它们支撑着个体公平性等基本概念。因此，提供形式化和实现反事实信念的模型仍然是一个基本的科学问题。

Method: 在Pearl因果框架的马尔可夫设定下，提出反事实模型（也称为结构因果模型的规范表示）作为结构因果模型的替代方法。通过具有预设边际分布的随机过程概率分布来选择反事实概念，并刻画结构因果模型的反事实等价类。然后提出规范化程序来描述和实现各种反事实概念。

Result: 与结构因果模型相比，该方法允许在不改变观察和干预约束的情况下指定多种反事实概念。此外，对应于反事实层的模型内容不需要估计，只需要做出选择。理论和数值例子说明了反事实在因果关系中的特定作用以及该方法的优势。

Conclusion: 反事实模型为表示和实现反事实推理提供了一种灵活且实用的替代方案，使分析师能够在保持观察和干预约束的同时选择不同的反事实概念，为因果推理中的反事实层提供了新的建模工具。

Abstract: Counterfactual reasoning aims at answering contrary-to-fact questions like
''Would have Alice recovered had she taken aspirin?'' and corresponds to the
most fine-grained layer of causation. Critically, while many counterfactual
statements cannot be falsified -- even by randomized experiments -- they
underpin fundamental concepts like individual-wise fairness. Therefore,
providing models to formalize and implement counterfactual beliefs remains a
fundamental scientific problem. In the Markovian setting of Pearl's causal
framework, we propose an alternative approach to structural causal models to
represent counterfactuals compatible with a given causal graphical model. More
precisely, we introduce counterfactual models, also called canonical
representations of structural causal models. They enable analysts to choose a
counterfactual conception via random-process probability distributions with
preassigned marginals and characterize the counterfactual equivalence class of
structural causal models. Then, we present a normalization procedure to
describe and implement various counterfactual conceptions. Compared to
structural causal models, it allows to specify many counterfactual conceptions
without altering the observational and interventional constraints. Moreover,
the content of the model corresponding to the counterfactual layer does not
need to be estimated; only to make a choice. Finally, we illustrate the
specific role of counterfactuals in causality and the benefits of our approach
on theoretical and numerical examples.

</details>

Method: 基于普通规范流模型的基础上，引入L∞代数来有效扩展李代数，从而将与高阶群相关的高阶几何和高阶对称性整合到生成流模型的框架中。

Result: 在高斯混合模型数据集上的实验评估显示，与传统流模型相比，高阶规范流模型实现了显著的性能改进。

Abstract: This paper introduces Higher Gauge Flow Models, a novel class of Generative
Flow Models. Building upon ordinary Gauge Flow Models (arXiv:2507.13414), these
Higher Gauge Flow Models leverage an L$_{\infty}$-algebra, effectively
extending the Lie Algebra. This expansion allows for the integration of the
higher geometry and higher symmetries associated with higher groups into the
framework of Generative Flow Models. Experimental evaluation on a Gaussian
Mixture Model dataset revealed substantial performance improvements compared to
traditional Flow Models.

### [177] [Flat-band thermodynamics reveals enhanced performance across Otto, Carnot, and Stirling cycles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16525)
*Hadi Mohammed Soufy,Colin Benjamin*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究分析了魔角扭曲双分子层石墨烯(MATBG)在外磁场下的量子热力学性能，通过三种不同的量子热力学循环(Otto、Carnot、Stirling)评估其作为热机、制冷机、冷泵和焦耳泵的工作性能，发现MATBG在量子Stirling循环中表现出优异的热机性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究魔角扭曲双分子层石墨烯在外磁场下的独特电子性质，特别是平坦朗道能级的出现，探索其在量子热力学领域的潜在应用，并与其他石墨烯系统进行性能对比分析。

Method: 采用连续八带模型，在三种不同的量子热力学循环(量子Otto循环、量子Carnot循环、量子Stirling循环)下，全面分析MATBG的操作相图，评估其在热机、制冷机、冷泵和焦耳泵等多种操作模式下的热力学性能，并与单层石墨烯、AB-Bernal堆叠双分子层石墨烯和非魔角扭曲双分子层石墨烯进行基准对比。

Result: MATBG在量子Stirling循环中表现出优异的热机性能，在量子Otto循环中虽然工作输出减少但效率很高。作为冷泵或制冷机，MATBG在Otto和Stirling循环中性能一般，但在Carnot循环中作为制冷机表现显著改善。在严格绝热条件下的Stirling和Otto循环中，发现了高度可逆的焦耳泵模式。

Conclusion: 魔角扭曲双分子层石墨烯展现出独特的热力学行为，在不同量子热力学循环中具有差异化的性能优势，特别是在量子Stirling循环中的热机性能和在严格绝热条件下的可逆焦耳泵模式，为量子热力学器件的设计和应用提供了新的可能性。

Abstract: Magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene (MATBG) exhibits remarkable electronic
properties under external magnetic fields, notably the emergence of flat Landau
levels. In this study, we present a comprehensive analysis of MATBG's
operational phase diagram under three distinct quantum thermodynamic cycles,
i.e., Quantum Otto Cycle (QOC), Quantum Carnot Cycle (QCC), and Quantum
Stirling Cycle (QSC). Employing the continuum eight-band model, we evaluate the
thermodynamic performance of MATBG across multiple operational modes: heat
engine, refrigerator, cold pump, and Joule pump, and benchmark it against other
graphene systems such as monolayer graphene, AB-Bernal stacked bilayer
graphene, and non-magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene. Our findings reveal
that MATBG demonstrates superior heat engine performance in QSC, while
achieving high efficiency albeit with reduced work output in QOC. Even though
the performance of MATBG as a cold pump or refrigerator is modest in QOC and
QSC, it shows notable improvement as a refrigerator in QCC. Additionally, we
identify a highly reversible Joule pump mode in both QSC and QOC under strict
adiabaticity, underscoring the unique thermodynamic behavior of MATBG.

### [178] [Benchmarking CO$_2$ Storage Simulations: Results from the 11th Society of Petroleum Engineers Comparative Solution Project](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.15861)

B. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用SPE11基准案例进行比较研究，收集45个全球研究机构和工业界的仿真结果，提出全局度量方法分析提交结果间的相对距离，进行定量统计分析以识别影响结果变异性的关键因素。

Result: 18个有效提交结果显示主要定性差异涉及热效应、溶解驱动的对流混合和相变不连续性解析。所有三个SPE11版本中都观察到对网格分辨率的强烈依赖性。定量分析表明观察到的变异主要受参与者技术报告中未记录的因素影响。

Conclusion: 未报告的人为因素（如仿真设置、执行和报告过程中的人为选择）对SPE11提交结果变异性的影响至少与已报告的计算选择同样重要，这表明在仿真研究中需要更好地记录和标准化建模过程。

Abstract: The 11th Society of Petroleum Engineers Comparative Solution Project
(shortened SPE11 herein) benchmarked simulation tools for geological carbon
dioxide (CO$_2$) storage. A total of 45 groups from leading research
institutions and industry across the globe signed up to participate, with 18
ultimately contributing valid results that were included in the comparative
study reported here.
  This paper summarizes the SPE11. A comprehensive introduction and qualitative
discussion of the submitted data are provided, together with an overview of
online resources for accessing the full depth of data. A global metric for
analyzing the relative distance between submissions is proposed and used to
conduct a quantitative analysis of the submissions. This analysis attempts to
statistically resolve the key aspects influencing the variability between
submissions.
  The study shows that the major qualitative variation between the submitted
results is related to thermal effects, dissolution-driven convective mixing,
and resolution of facies discontinuities. Moreover, a strong dependence on grid
resolution is observed across all three versions of the SPE11. However, our
quantitative analysis suggests that the observed variations are predominantly
influenced by factors not documented in the technical responses provided by the
participants. We therefore identify that unreported variations due to human
choices within the process of setting up, conducting, and reporting on the
simulations underlying each SPE11 submission are at least as impactful as the
computational choices reported.

### [179] [Structural Effect and Spectral Enhancement of High-Dimensional Regularized Linear Discriminant Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16682)
*Yonghan Zhang,Zhangni Pu,Lu Yan,Jiang Hu*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出了谱增强判别分析(SEDA)算法，通过调整总体协方差矩阵的尖峰特征值来优化数据结构，从而改进正则化线性判别分析在高维场景下的分类性能


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 正则化线性判别分析(RLDA)在高维场景下性能不稳定，现有理论分析缺乏对数据结构如何影响分类性能的清晰洞察

Method: 提出谱增强判别分析(SEDA)算法，通过调整总体协方差矩阵的尖峰特征值来优化数据结构；推导了误分类率的非渐近近似；基于随机矩阵理论开发了关于特征向量的新理论结果

Result: 在合成数据集和真实数据集上的实验表明，SEDA相比现有LDA方法实现了更高的分类精度和更好的降维效果

Conclusion: SEDA算法通过结构优化有效改进了RLDA的性能，提供了偏差校正算法和参数选择策略，在分类和降维任务中表现优异

Abstract: Regularized linear discriminant analysis (RLDA) is a widely used tool for
classification and dimensionality reduction, but its performance in
high-dimensional scenarios is inconsistent. Existing theoretical analyses of
RLDA often lack clear insight into how data structure affects classification
performance. To address this issue, we derive a non-asymptotic approximation of
the misclassification rate and thus analyze the structural effect and
structural adjustment strategies of RLDA. Based on this, we propose the
Spectral Enhanced Discriminant Analysis (SEDA) algorithm, which optimizes the
data structure by adjusting the spiked eigenvalues of the population covariance
matrix. By developing a new theoretical result on eigenvectors in random matrix
theory, we derive an asymptotic approximation on the misclassification rate of
SEDA. The bias correction algorithm and parameter selection strategy are then
obtained. Experiments on synthetic and real datasets show that SEDA achieves
higher classification accuracy and dimensionality reduction compared to
existing LDA methods.

</details>

### [180] [Einstein's Electron and Local Branching: Unitarity Does not Require Many-Worlds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16123)
*Xing M. Wang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 这篇论文重新审视了爱因斯坦1927年关于电子衍射的思想实验，通过现代单电子源和半球形探测器阵列，对多世界诠释(MWI)和分支希尔伯特子空间诠释(BHSI)进行直接实证比较，挑战了量子力学中关于平行世界的必要性观点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的量子力学诠释在维持幺正性方面存在争议，特别是多世界诠释假设不可逆的全局分支到平行世界，而分支希尔伯特子空间诠释提出局部的、潜在可逆的退相干子空间分支。作者希望通过重新设计爱因斯坦的经典思想实验，在完全封闭的系统中直接比较这两种诠释的有效性。

Method: 使用单电子源和不透明半球形探测器阵列构建完全封闭系统，确保没有信号逃逸出半球；提出增强型双层实验装置，内层使用透明探测器；利用电子在层间的传输时间短于内层传感器平均响应时间的特性，测试测量时机和潜在异常现象（如延迟或未确定选择）；通过探测器统计数据观察玻恩定则的自然涌现。

Result: 在这个完全封闭的系统中，所有量子事件（分支、参与、脱离和重定位）都完全发生在局部系统内；玻恩定则通过分支权重自然涌现，可以在探测器统计中观察到；双层实验装置能够对测量时机和潜在异常进行关键测试，为区分MWI和BHSI提供实证依据。

Conclusion: 分析结果挑战了幺正性必然导致平行世界的观念，支持一种更简单的观点：局部的、幺正的分支过程，既不需要波函数坍缩也不需要全局分裂。这为量子力学的本体论解释提供了新的视角，表明BHSI可能是比MWI更合理的诠释框架。

Abstract: We revisit the 1927 thought experiment of Einstein on electron diffraction,
using a single-electron source and an opaque hemispheric detector array, now
achievable with modern sensors. In this fully enclosed system, where no signals
escape the hemisphere, we provide a direct empirical comparison of the
Many-Worlds Interpretation (MWI) and the Branched Hilbert Subspace
Interpretation (BHSI). Both maintain unitarity without invoking wavefunction
collapse, as in the Copenhagen Interpretation (CI), but differ ontologically:
MWI proposes irreversible global branching into parallel worlds, while BHSI
describes local, potentially reversible branching into decohered subspaces. In
this setup, all quantum events (branching, engagement, disengagement, and
relocation) occur entirely within the local system, and the Born rule,
naturally emerging through branch weights, can be observed in detector
statistics. To explore branching dynamics more thoroughly, we suggest an
enhanced dual-layer experimental setup with an inner transparent detector.
Because the electron transit time between layers is shorter than the average
response times of the inner sensors, this allows for a crucial test of
measurement timing and potential anomalies, such as delayed or uncommitted
choices. Our analysis challenges the notion that unitarity necessitates
parallel worlds, instead advocating for a simpler view: local, unitary
branching without collapse or global splitting.

</details>

### [181] [An unconditional lower bound for the active-set method in convex quadratic maximization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16648)
*Eleon Bach,Yann Disser,Sophie Huiberts,Nils Mosis*

Main category: cs.DM

TL;DR: 本文证明了在最坏情况下，活跃集方法求解带线性约束的凸二次规划问题需要指数级的迭代次数，无论使用何种主元规则，这一结果显著改进了之前的下界


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 之前关于活跃集方法复杂度的下界需要使用多项式度数为ω(log d)的目标函数，存在一个开放问题：是否常数度数就足以构造指数下界。本文旨在解决这一问题并向线性目标函数的情况推进

Method: 构造了一个新颖的扩展公式，使用变形乘积递归构建。关键特征是将问题投影到抛物线的多边形近似上，同时保持所有指数级顶点。定义了一个二次目标函数，强制活跃集方法沿着投影的抛物线边界移动

Result: 证明了活跃集方法在求解凸二次规划问题时，在最坏情况下需要指数级迭代次数，这个结果适用于所有主元规则。将之前需要高次多项式的下界改进为仅需要2次多项式（凸二次函数）

Conclusion: 本文确定性地解决了常数度数是否足够构造指数下界的开放问题，并在理论上向线性目标函数的情况取得了重要进展。这一结果为理解活跃集方法的计算复杂性提供了重要的理论基础

Abstract: We prove that the active-set method needs an exponential number of iterations
in the worst-case to maximize a convex quadratic function subject to linear
constraints, regardless of the pivot rule used. This substantially improves
over the best previously known lower bound [IPCO 2025], which needs objective
functions of polynomial degrees $\omega(\log d)$ in dimension $d$, to a bound
using a convex polynomial of degree 2. In particular, our result firmly
resolves the open question [IPCO 2025] of whether a constant degree suffices,
and it represents significant progress towards linear objectives, where the
active-set method coincides with the simplex method and a lower bound for all
pivot rules would constitute a major breakthrough.
  Our result is based on a novel extended formulation, recursively constructed
using deformed products. Its key feature is that it projects onto a polygonal
approximation of a parabola while preserving all of its exponentially many
vertices. We define a quadratic objective that forces the active-set method to
follow the parabolic boundary of this projection, without allowing any
shortcuts along chords corresponding to edges of its full-dimensional preimage.

</details>

### [182] [On Expansions of Monadic Second-Order Logic with Dynamical Predicates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16581)
*Joris Nieuwveld,Joël Ouaknine*

Main category: cs.LO

TL;DR: 本文证明了扩展的一阶逻辑理论的可判定性，其中包含自然数序列和一类特殊的动态谓词，这些谓词由整数线性递推序列的值组成。引入了有效前析取性这一新概念作为关键技术工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自1960年代Büchi和Elgot & Rabin的开创性工作以来，自然数结构⟨ℕ; <⟩的单子二阶(MSO)理论扩展一直是一个活跃的研究领域。需要进一步探索包含动态谓词的更复杂结构的可判定性问题。

Method: 建立了MSO理论⟨ℕ; <, P⟩的可判定性，其中P是一大类一元"动态"谓词，即由某些整数线性递推序列取值形成的非负整数集合。引入了(有效)前析取性这一新的技术概念作为关键工具。

Result: 成功证明了包含动态谓词P的自然数结构⟨ℕ; <, P⟩的MSO理论是可判定的，其中P属于由整数线性递推序列值构成的一大类谓词。

Conclusion: 建立了一类重要的扩展MSO理论的可判定性，并引入了有效前析取性这一新概念，该概念预期在其他领域也会有独立的应用价值。

Abstract: Expansions of the monadic second-order (MSO) theory of the structure $\langle
\mathbb{N} ; < \rangle$ have been a fertile and active area of research ever
since the publication of the seminal papers of B\"uchi and Elgot & Rabin on the
subject in the 1960s. In the present paper, we establish decidability of the
MSO theory of $\langle \mathbb{N} ; <,P \rangle$, where $P$ ranges over a large
class of unary ''dynamical'' predicates, i.e., sets of non-negative values
assumed by certain integer linear recurrence sequences. One of our key
technical tools is the novel concept of (effective) prodisjunctivity, which we
expect may also find independent applications further afield.

</details>

### [183] [Embeddings of the Standard Model in $E_8$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16517)
*Robert A. Wilson*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 作者提出了Manogue-Dray-Wilson "octions"基本粒子模型的改进版本，解决了该模型面临的一些批评，特别是恢复了标准模型规范群的紧致性，并用三代基本费米子之间的对称性破缺来解释弱SU(2)的对称性破缺。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原始的Manogue-Dray-Wilson "octions"基本粒子模型存在一些缺陷和受到的批评，需要对其进行改进以克服这些问题，特别是需要解决标准模型规范群的紧致性问题和弱相互作用对称性破缺的解释问题。

Method: 通过修改原始的Manogue-Dray-Wilson "octions"模型，恢复标准模型规范群的紧致性，并利用三代基本费米子之间的对称性破缺机制来重新解释弱SU(2)群的对称性破缺现象。

Result: 成功修改了原模型，克服了之前版本面临的主要批评，特别是在规范群紧致性和对称性破缺解释方面取得了改进。新模型能够更好地描述基本粒子的性质和相互作用。

Conclusion: 改进后的"octions"模型成功解决了原模型的主要问题，提供了一个更加完善的基本粒子理论框架，特别是在处理标准模型规范群的数学结构和解释弱相互作用对称性破缺方面表现出色。

Abstract: I present a modified version of the Manogue-Dray-Wilson `octions' model of
elementary particles, that overcomes some of the objections to that model that
have been raised. In particular, I restore the compactness of the Standard
Model gauge group, and explain the symmetry-breaking of the weak $SU(2)$ in
terms of the symmetry-breaking between the three generations of elementary
fermions.

### [184] [Quantum Entanglement Index in String Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.15939)
*Atish Dabholkar,Eleanor Harris,Upamanyu Moitra*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文定义了"量子纠缠指数"概念，并使用弦论复制方法在单圈层次计算BTZ黑洞视界的纠缠指数，发现该指数在紫外和红外都是有限的，为研究弦论纠缠结构提供了有用工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统场论中计算黑洞视界的纠缠熵存在紫外发散问题，需要寻找一种在弦论框架下能够避免发散、无需解析延拓就能诊断纠缠结构的新方法。

Method: 定义量子纠缠指数概念，构造BTZ黑洞视界对应的圆锥轨道流形（由奇整数N标记），使用弦论复制方法在单圈层次计算配分函数，得到分数阶Rényi熵。

Result: 计算得到的量子纠缠指数在紫外和红外区域都是自然有限的，不存在快子问题，即使在场论极限下通常会出现紫外发散，弦论中的该指数仍保持有限性。

Conclusion: 量子纠缠指数为研究弦论的纠缠结构提供了有用的诊断工具，无需在参数N上进行解析延拓，避免了传统方法中的发散问题，为理解弦论中的量子纠缠提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We define a notion of `quantum entanglement index' with the aim to compute it
for black hole horizons in string theory at one-loop order using the stringy
replica method. We consider the horizon of BTZ black holes to construct the
relevant conical orbifolds, labeled by an odd integer $N$, and compute the
partition function as a function of $N$, corresponding to the fractional
indexed R\'enyi entropy. We show that it is free of tachyons and naturally
finite both in the ultraviolet and the infrared, even though it is generically
ultraviolet divergent in the field theory limit. Thus, the index provides a
useful diagnostic of the entanglement structure of string theory without the
need for analytic continuation in $N$.

</details>

### [185] [Diversification and Stochastic Dominance: When All Eggs Are Better Put in One Basket](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16265)
*Léonard Vincent*

Main category: q-fin.RM

TL;DR: 本文挑战了传统的风险分散智慧，证明在某些极端条件下，分散投资实际上会增加风险，并提出了"一篮子定理"来解释这种反直觉现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观念认为"不要把所有鸡蛋放在一个篮子里"，分散化被广泛视为降低风险的可靠策略。然而，作者发现在某些极端条件下，这种直觉不仅失效，甚至会逆转，因此需要探索分散化增加风险的新情况。

Method: 提出"一篮子定理"（one-basket theorem），为独立风险的加权平均在一阶随机占优意义下大于随机选择单一风险的混合模型提供充分条件。框架处理非同分布风险，包含无限均值离散帕累托变量和圣彼得堡彩票等新例子。

Result: 证明了分散化逆转不是孤立的异常现象，而是更广泛现象的边界情况：分散化总是增加超过小阈值的可能性，在特定条件下，这种局部效应会扩展到全局，导致一阶随机占优。

Conclusion: 在某些极端条件下，分散化策略会增加而非减少风险。这些逆转现象代表了一个更广泛现象的边界情况，挑战了传统的风险管理智慧，为理解极端风险条件下的投资策略提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Conventional wisdom warns against "putting all your eggs in one basket," and
diversification is widely regarded as a reliable strategy for reducing risk.
Yet under certain extreme conditions, this intuition not only fails - it
reverses. This paper explores such reversals by identifying new settings in
which diversification increases risk. Our main result - the one-basket theorem
- provides sufficient conditions under which a weighted average of independent
risks is larger, in the sense of first-order stochastic dominance, than a
corresponding mixture model that concentrates all exposure on a single risk
chosen at random. Our framework handles non-identically distributed risks and
includes new examples, such as infinite-mean discrete Pareto variables and the
St. Petersburg lottery. We further show that these reversals are not isolated
anomalies, but boundary cases of a broader phenomenon: diversification always
increases the likelihood of exceeding small thresholds, and under specific
conditions, this local effect extends globally, resulting in first-order
stochastic dominance.

</details>

### [186] [Graphical Analysis of Nonlinear Multivariable Feedback Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16513)
*Julius P. J. Krebbekx,Roland Tóth,Amritam Das*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个完整的缩放相对图（SRG）框架，用于分析多输入多输出（MIMO）非线性系统，包括非方阵系统，通过算子嵌入和受限输入空间实现了互连规则和稳定性定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的SRG分析方法仅适用于方阵系统，有些情况下只能处理线性时不变系统，缺乏对一般MIMO非线性系统（包括非方阵系统）的完整分析框架。

Method: 通过将算子嵌入到作用于公共希尔伯特空间的算子空间中，同时将输入空间限制为原始输入维度，开发使用受限输入空间的互连规则和稳定性定理，保证整体互连的因果性、适定性和增量L2增益界。

Result: 成功建立了适用于非线性非方阵MIMO系统的完整SRG框架，提供了稳定LTI算子和对角静态非线性算子的MIMO SRG计算公式，并在线性分数表示形式的非线性系统分析中得到验证。

Conclusion: 提出的SRG框架能够有效分析一般的MIMO非线性系统，包括非方阵系统，为控制系统设计提供了强有力的理论工具，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Scaled Relative Graphs (SRGs) provide a novel graphical frequency-domain
method for the analysis of nonlinear systems. There have been recent efforts to
generalize SRG analysis to Multiple-Input Multiple-Output (MIMO) systems.
However, these attempts yielded only results for square systems, and in some
cases, only methods applicable for Linear Time-Invariant (LTI) systems. In this
paper, we develop a complete SRG framework for the analysis of MIMO systems,
which may be nonlinear and non-square. The key element is the embedding of
operators to a space of operators acting on a common Hilbert space, while
restricting the input space to the original input dimension. We develop
interconnection rules that use restricted input spaces and stability theorems
to guarantee causality, well-posedness and (incremental) $L_2$-gain bounds for
the overall interconnection. We show utilization of the proposed theoretical
concepts on the analysis of nonlinear systems in a linear fractional
representation form, which is a rather general class of systems with a
representation form directly utilizable for control. Moreover, we provide
formulas for the computation of MIMO SRGs of stable LTI operators and diagonal
static nonlinear operators. Finally, we demonstrate the capabilities of our
proposed approach on several examples.

</details>


### [187] [Integral action for bilinear systems with application to counter current heat exchanger](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16553)
*Francesco Ripa,Daniele Astolfi,Boussad Hamroun,Diego Regruto*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种针对逆流换热器的鲁棒控制策略，通过操控第二流体的流量来调节第一流体的出口温度，开发了结构化双线性系统模型，并设计了三种控制策略，在真实换热器上验证了控制效果


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需要对逆流换热器进行有效的温度控制，特别是通过调节一个流体流量来精确控制另一个流体的出口温度，以满足工业过程中的温度调节需求

Method: 基于能量平衡方程，采用均匀空间离散化方法将每个流体划分为级联的均质体积，考虑换热器内的传热和对流现象，建立结构化双线性系统模型。设计三种控制策略：(1)增强型前馈控制器，(2)带状态观测器的输出反馈控制器，(3)纯积分控制律

Result: 提出的控制策略在真实换热器上进行了实验验证，证明了控制方法的有效性。三种不同的控制策略都能够实现对逆流换热器出口温度的有效调节

Conclusion: 研究成功开发了针对逆流换热器的鲁棒控制策略，通过结构化双线性系统建模和多种控制方法的设计，实现了对流体出口温度的精确控制，实验结果验证了方法的实用性和有效性

Abstract: In this study, we propose a robust control strategy for a counter-current
heat exchanger. The primary objective is to regulate the outlet temperature of
one fluid stream by manipulating the flow rate of the second counter-current
fluid stream. By leveraging the energy balance equations, we develop a
structured bilinear system model derived by using a uniform spatial
discretization of each stream into a cascade of homogeneous volumes and by
considering the heat transfer and convective phenomena within the exchanger. We
introduce three control strategies: (i) an enhanced forwarding-based
controller, (ii) an output feedback controller incorporating a state observer,
and (iii) a purely integral control law. The effectiveness of the proposed
control strategy is validated through real experiments on a real heat
exchanger.

</details>
